About the job
Description

Position Summary

Data Analysis Trainee assists in analysis activities including data setup, data searches, feature identification and marking.
Primary Responsibilities
Safety shall always be the top priority
Work in a team environment collaborating and sharing knowledge and experiences
Learn the responsibilities and required tasks of a Level I Data Analysis.
Accomplish all requirements of a Level I Data Analysis qualification and pass respective evaluation.
Interpret industry documentation on ILI tools and pipeline integrity
Under the supervision of a Data Analysis Level II or higher perform data preparation and processing of ILI data
Under the supervision of a Data Analysis Level II or higher perform feature categorization, evaluation and marking
Performs other assigned tasks

Requirements

Degree or diploma in engineering, science or technical discipline; or equivalent experience preferred
Strong work ethic with a can-do attitude
Proficient with operating relevant customized and shrink-wrap computer software applications
Understanding of Microsoft Suite Products.
Demonstrated ability to deliver timely, accurate, and complete results
Requires a strong ability to sustain focus on one or more tasks while avoiding distractions.
Willingness to handle repetitive tasks
Requires pattern recognition and spatial thinking skill.
Must be customer focused, have an excellent attention to detail and a strong ability to work in a team environment
About the job
Bombardier is a global leader, creating innovative and game-changing planes. Our products and services provide world-class transportation experiences that set new standards in passenger comfort, energy, efficiency, reliability and safety. We are a global organization focused on working together with a team spirit.

In your role, you will

Analyze the needs of internal customers and generate appropriate project plans.
Extract, import, process and document source data.
Implement data sets for Power BI visibilities
Be responsible for the design, implementation and documentation of new web applications
Support and improve existing IT systems (web applications and desktop).
Provide leadership in the development of new tools up until implementation.
Actively collaborate in continuous improvement activities and initiatives with the team.


As our ideal candidate

 You have a Bachelor in Computer Science or Software Engineering or other relevant experience. 
 You have acquired a minimum of three (3) years of experience. 
 You have a very good knowledge in several of the following areas: 
 Transact-SQL 
 SQL Server (SSIS, SSAS, SSRS) 
 BI – datawarehouse, PowerBI 
 Microsoft Azure 
 ASP.NET (C#) 
 Database modeling 
 You have the skills to build partnerships with key players from different departments. 
 You are organized and meet your commitments 
 You are independent and your teamwork is recognized 
 Your flexibility allows you to work on multiple tasks / projects simultaneously 
 You are bilingual (French and English)

 Envie de développer votre carrière avec nous? 

Joignez-vous à BBA pour faire partie d’une équipe de personnes de talent animées d’une passion de réussir et d’une volonté de se dépasser afin d’offrir le meilleur à leurs clients. Vous aurez également la chance de réaliser des projets stimulants et formateurs. Vous serez accompagné,e par des gens d’expérience qui ont à cœur le développement de leurs collègues et qui n’hésiteront pas à partager leurs connaissances.

Chez BBA, vous trouverez une ambiance de travail stimulante, conviviale, amusante et inclusive. Nous misons sur la complémentarité de nos équipes et offrons à nos employé.e.s un environnement propice à leur épanouissement personnel et professionnel.

 Avec nous, vous aurez l’occasion de… 

 Concevoir et développer des projets en analyse avancée de données et en intelligence artificielle (IA) pour nos clients industriels et manufacturiers. 
 Soutenir nos clients dans la mise en valeur de leurs données en leur proposant des solutions novatrices fondées sur différents concepts comme l’apprentissage machine et la maintenance prédictive. 
 Avoir un impact sur les entreprises de demain en participant à leur transformation numérique. 
 Travailler dans une équipe stimulante qui vous pousse à vous dépasser et à toujours en apprendre plus. 
 Diriger des équipes de projet en tant que leader technique en vous appuyant sur votre expérience et vos compétences. 
 Développer un réseau de contacts et une expérience concrète sur le terrain ainsi que faire de la représentation pour des clients. 
 Participer à la gestion, à l’implantation de systèmes, de logiciels utilitaires et autres progiciels industriels. 
 Assurer la qualité du service professionnel et une bonne relation avec les clients.

À propos de BBA

Depuis plus de 40 ans, nous repoussons les limites du génie pour servir nos clients de l’industrie de l’Énergie et des ressources naturelles. Chez BBA, nous développons des solutions novatrices, flexibles et durables – de la stratégie à l’exécution.

BBA est l’une des plus importantes firmes de génie-conseil privées au Canada qui s’appuie sur un réseau de 15 bureaux. Nos équipes travaillent en collaboration pour réaliser des projets qui façonnent l’industrie de demain à l’échelle locale, nationale et internationale.

La passion et l’excellence de nos gens font de BBA un Employeur de choix au Canada , et l’une des Sociétés les mieux gérées .

Nos talents sont uniques, et nous nous engageons à offrir un milieu de travail où l’on peut être soi-même . À l’exception du titre du poste qui a été féminisé pour optimiser sa découvrabilité, cette offre d’emploi a été rédigée en écriture épicène.

Apprenez-en davantage sur nous en visitant notre page LinkedIn et rejoignez les réseaux de nos spécialistes en attraction de talents pour une occasion de discuter de vive voix.

About the job
Inspirantes, ingénieuses, animées de l’esprit d’entreprise : voilà ce qui décrit bien nos équipes d’exception. Donnez une vocation à votre passion en rejoignant une culture qui s’épanouit face au changement.

Faites votre marque au sein du Groupe des normes professionnelles en certification - Conception des méthodes de certification à titre de directeur(trice). Cette équipe diversifiée de professionnels mise sur son expertise technique et sectorielle pour contribuer, à l’interne, au succès de notre pratique de certification et de comptabilité. En tant que conseiller de confiance, vous jouerez un rôle influent en matière de nouvelles tendances et de changements pour vous assurer que nos membres répondent aux normes les plus rigoureuses du secteur.

Notre identité canadienne est pour nous une source de fierté. Nous sommes un cabinet de comptabilité, de fiscalité et de services-conseils de premier plan au Canada qui propose des stratégies et des solutions aux entreprises. Entrepreneurs dans l’âme, les membres talentueux de notre équipe voient les obstacles comme des occasions de se dépasser et transforment les façons de faire sur le marché des petites et moyennes entreprises.

Responsabilités

Promouvoir l’importance du contrôle de la qualité auprès des associés, des directeurs et des autres membres du cabinet et jouer un rôle central dans les initiatives du cabinet visant la qualité.
Appuyer la conception et la mise à jour des politiques et des lignes directrices encadrant les missions du cabinet de même que ses protocoles de comptabilité et d’audit.
Se tenir au courant des changements dans la profession en effectuant des recherches et en prenant part à des activités et à des séances de formation organisées dans le secteur.
Contribuer à la conception et faciliter la mise en œuvre des formations en certification dans le cadre des programmes de perfectionnement interne exhaustifs de MNP.
Entretenir des liens et des échanges professionnels avec les équipes de certification et de comptabilité du cabinet et avec ses équipes de direction.
Acquérir une solide compréhension des services de MNP ainsi que des entreprises et des secteurs servis par le cabinet.
Prendre part à l’élaboration de nouvelles idées et méthodes pour améliorer les procédures de travail.
Optimiser les effectifs afin qu’un travail complet et exact soit livré dans le respect des échéances.
Fournir un mentorat aux membres de l’équipe, les motiver et les encadrer pour qu’ils puissent se perfectionner et s’épanouir grâce à des objectifs clairs, à une rétroaction régulière et à une résolution rapide des problèmes de rendement, en plus de procéder aux évaluations de rendement.
Être disposé à se déplacer, au besoin.

Expérience de la conception et la mise en œuvre de procédures d’audit fondées sur le risque et le caractère significatif

MesAvantages@MNP 

Offrant un potentiel de revenus élevés, MNP est fier de proposer des avantages taillés sur mesure qui sont à l’image de notre culture d’exception et qui favorisent un mode de vie équilibré, le tout pour aider ses membres à s’épanouir, tant au bureau que dans leur vie personnelle. Vous profiterez d’un salaire de base généreux, de vacances, de quatre congés personnels payés par année, d’un régime collectif de retraite avec cotisations égalées à 4 %, de produits d’épargne volontaire, de programmes de primes, d’avantages sociaux à la carte, de ressources en santé mentale, d’un accès exclusif à des rabais et à des avantages indirects, d’une aide au perfectionnement professionnel, de cours offerts à l’interne par l’intermédiaire de MNP University, d’un code vestimentaire adapté à vos tâches, d’activités sociales organisées par le cabinet, et plus encore!

About the job
Who is Allstate:
Allstate Insurance Company of Canada is a leading home and auto insurer focused on providing its customers prevention and protection products and services for every stage of life. The company is proud to have been named a Best Employer in Canada for nine consecutive years and prioritizes supporting employees and fostering an inclusive, welcoming corporate culture. Allstate is committed to making a positive difference in the communities in which it operates through partnerships with charitable organizations, employee giving and volunteerism. Serving Canadians since 1953, Allstate strives to provide reassurance with its "You’re in Good Hands®" promise.
Through our Employee Value Proposition, Opportunity, Flexibility, Community, Diversity and Family, we have worked hard to develop and nurture a culture where employees feel valued, experience personal growth, have career options and truly enjoy the work they do. 

Role Designation: Hybrid (Once a month in office)

Job description: 
Our team is growing and we are actively looking to hire a Senior Data/Claims Analyst to join our team! The Claims Intelligence team within Distribution Design and Delivery collaborates with stakeholders across the organization, leveraging data and analytics to deliver strategies and solutions that drive operational efficiency and profitable growth. We are looking for a Senior Data/Claims Analyst experienced with data extraction, transformation, and visualization who can act as a consultant—quickly understanding business problems and effectively communicating insights to our stakeholders

Accountabilities:
Develop, design, and productionize reports/dashboards to support the measurement of key KPIs for business partners in claims
Assist in establishing data pipelines to feed into new and existing reports
Develop a strong understanding of ACG claim processes and data to be able to untangle the story behind our data and provide our stakeholders with actionable insights
Lead efforts on ad-hoc investigations into irregular claims patterns and cost trendshelping support our stakeholders’ decision-making
Build strong relationsihps with, and act as a consultant to the Reserving, Finance and Claims departments to support ongoing and new analyses
As a Senior Data/Claims Analyst, independently lead analytics projects and provide technical support to junior analysts.

Qualifications:
4+ years in an analytics-focused role
3+ years of experience in manipulating, summarizing, and analyzing data using SQL and/or SAS
3+ years of experience in a data visualization tool, preferably Power BI or Tableau
Exceptional analytical and critical thinking skills
Must be able to take ownership of, and lead analytics projects from beginning to end
Must be able to analyze complex data with high accuracy, be open minded towards change, anticipate stakeholder needs and work with others to identify and resolve issues
Must be able to coordinate various priorities under time pressure and ensure alignment to corporate objectives
Strong communication (written and verbal), collaboration and relationship-building skills

Bonus qualification:
Understanding of the insurance industry and general insurance concepts
Experience with claims data and processes
Any analytics specific certification or education is plus
Post-Secondary degree in a quantitative study such as statistics, actuarial science, economics, computer science or education in insurance claims or equivalent

Allstate Canada Group has policies and practices that provide workplace accommodations. If you require accommodation, please let us know and we will work with you to meet your needs.
About the job
Inspirantes, ingénieuses, animées de l’esprit d’entreprise : voilà ce qui décrit bien nos équipes d’exception. Donnez une vocation à votre passion en rejoignant une culture qui s’épanouit face au changement.

Faites votre marque au sein du Groupe des normes professionnelles en certification - Conception des méthodes de certification à titre de directeur(trice). Cette équipe diversifiée de professionnels mise sur son expertise technique et sectorielle pour contribuer, à l’interne, au succès de notre pratique de certification et de comptabilité. En tant que conseiller de confiance, vous jouerez un rôle influent en matière de nouvelles tendances et de changements pour vous assurer que nos membres répondent aux normes les plus rigoureuses du secteur.

Notre identité canadienne est pour nous une source de fierté. Nous sommes un cabinet de comptabilité, de fiscalité et de services-conseils de premier plan au Canada qui propose des stratégies et des solutions aux entreprises. Entrepreneurs dans l’âme, les membres talentueux de notre équipe voient les obstacles comme des occasions de se dépasser et transforment les façons de faire sur le marché des petites et moyennes entreprises.

Responsabilités

Promouvoir l’importance du contrôle de la qualité auprès des associés, des directeurs et des autres membres du cabinet et jouer un rôle central dans les initiatives du cabinet visant la qualité.
Appuyer la conception et la mise à jour des politiques et des lignes directrices encadrant les missions du cabinet de même que ses protocoles de comptabilité et d’audit.
Se tenir au courant des changements dans la profession en effectuant des recherches et en prenant part à des activités et à des séances de formation organisées dans le secteur.
Contribuer à la conception et faciliter la mise en œuvre des formations en certification dans le cadre des programmes de perfectionnement interne exhaustifs de MNP.
Entretenir des liens et des échanges professionnels avec les équipes de certification et de comptabilité du cabinet et avec ses équipes de direction.
Acquérir une solide compréhension des services de MNP ainsi que des entreprises et des secteurs servis par le cabinet.
Prendre part à l’élaboration de nouvelles idées et méthodes pour améliorer les procédures de travail.
Optimiser les effectifs afin qu’un travail complet et exact soit livré dans le respect des échéances.
Fournir un mentorat aux membres de l’équipe, les motiver et les encadrer pour qu’ils puissent se perfectionner et s’épanouir grâce à des objectifs clairs, à une rétroaction régulière et à une résolution rapide des problèmes de rendement, en plus de procéder aux évaluations de rendement.
Être disposé à se déplacer, au besoin.


Compétences et expérience 

Minimum de deux ans d'expérience à titre de comptable principal(e) dans le service de certification d’un des sept grands cabinets comptables et expérience antérieure en certification
Expérience de la conception et la mise en œuvre de procédures d’audit fondées sur le risque et le caractère significatif
Capacité de communiquer et d'écrire en Français et en anglais 
Connaissance des
Contrôles internes et de leur application
Diverses normes comptables (p. ex., NCECF, NCOSBL, NCSP)
Interprétation et application des normes de certification (p. ex., NCA et/ou ISA)
Compétences en rédaction technique et en gestion de projets; compréhension des principes commerciaux, de gestion et d’expansion des affaires s’appliquant à un cabinet

Offrant un potentiel de revenus élevés, MNP est fier de proposer des avantages taillés sur mesure qui sont à l’image de notre culture d’exception et qui favorisent un mode de vie équilibré, le tout pour aider ses membres à s’épanouir, tant au bureau que dans leur vie personnelle. Vous profiterez d’un salaire de base généreux, de vacances, de quatre congés personnels payés par année, d’un régime collectif de retraite avec cotisations égalées à 4 %, de produits d’épargne volontaire, de programmes de primes, d’avantages sociaux à la carte, de ressources en santé mentale, d’un accès exclusif à des rabais et à des avantages indirects, d’une aide au perfectionnement professionnel, de cours offerts à l’interne par l’intermédiaire de MNP University, d’un code vestimentaire adapté à vos tâches, d’activités sociales organisées par le cabinet, et plus encore!

 Work arrangements defined: 
Resident – you will work at your primary in-office headquarters on all scheduled workdays.
Hybrid 8 – you will work a minimum of 8 days per month at your primary in-office headquarters (typically 2 days per week). The remaining days will be remote within British Columbia. 
Hybrid 10 – you will work a minimum of 10 days per month at your primary in-office headquarters (typically one week in/one week out or up to 3 days per week). The remaining days will be remote within British Columbia. 
Mobile – you will work remotely or in the field on scheduled workdays within British Columbia, with the requirement to be at your primary on-site headquarters by exception only.

About Agoda

Agoda is an online travel booking platform for accommodations, flights, and more. We build and deploy cutting-edge technology that connects travelers with more than 3.6 million accommodations globally. Based in Asia and part of Booking Holdings, our 6,000+ employees representing 90+ nationalities foster a work environment rich in diversity, creativity, and collaboration. We innovate through a culture of experimentation and ownership, enhancing the ability for our customers to experience the world.

THIS ROLE IS BASED IN BANGKOK, THAILAND (WITH RELOCATION PROVIDED)

Location: Bangkok, Thailand (*Not open for remote work.)

Get to Know our Team:

As part of the Supply Analytics, you will be responsible for identifying new partners and opportunities, cultivating a relationship with them, and working together with them to deliver the best outcome for our end customers. You would also be responsible with managing the day-to-day interaction with the partner and working closely with other teams within Agoda to ensure the partners needs are met.

We design tailored business and product solutions with our partners and help them generate measurable value. Members of our team are empowered and supported to grow their market(s) or accounts. We develop win-win relationships and leverage Agoda’s unique accommodations portfolio and tech solutions to bring our partners the advantages they seek. Utilizing our strong brand and resources, we build new channels to increase the visibility of Agoda, introduce more travelers to our great products and service and deliver significant revenues to the overall business.

The Opportunity: 

As an Analyst/Senior Analyst, you will report directly to either the Senior Manager or Associate Director within the Supply Department and this will be an individual contributor role. You will be responsible and fully empowered to work with the partners on the ground. You will be supported by a team within the Supply department and work closely with other Team members within Agoda.

In this Role, you’ll get to:

Translate internal briefs into analytical projects (to include refining the initial brief and asking the ‘right questions’, working through potential hypotheses and storyboarding the output)
Use and analyze data from multiple large-scale data warehouses and present statistically strong analysis to a wide range of business stakeholders
Proactively identify opportunities for growth within supply and the wider business
Drive new analytical initiatives and projects aimed at improving organizational efficiency and shaping Agoda supply
Identify, support, and lead projects aimed at scaling up the way the Supply organization leverages on data, insights, and intelligence
Automate manual operational processes and present back on time savings gained through modernization of business operations

What you’ll Need to Succeed:

At least 3-5+ years of experience working as an Analyst with experience in analytics/data science/insights/strategy/BI
Advanced working knowledge and hands-on experience in SQL
Strong knowledge and hands-on experience in data visualization tools such as Tableau (preferably) 
Expert domain of data analysis and data visualization tools and software such as Excel, Python (or R)
Bachelor’s degree ideally in a business or quantitative subject (e.g. computer science, mathematics, engineering, science, economics or finance)
A good understanding of statistical modelling knowledge or any machine learning technique knowledge (such as hypothesis testing, regression, logistic regression, random forest, etc.)
Good stakeholder management experience. Comfortable presenting to senior leadership and C-suite
Experience in conducting A/B testing experimentation
Strong experience in finding data insights and provide business recommendation to the business
A hacker’s mindset – the ability to build simple but clever and elegant solutions to new problems within significant resource, operational and time constraints through deep understanding of the business, creative problem solving, and a wide range of expertise in data, analytics, automation, programming, and prototyping
Excellent communicator with superior written, verbal, presentation and interpersonal communication skills
Data driven in both decision making and performance measurement
Extreme comfort in ambiguous, fast-paced environment
Ability to multi-task, prioritize and coordinate resources

It’s Great if you Have: 

MBA or Masters in a quantitative subject (e.g. computer science, mathematics, engineering, science, economics or finance)
Program management certifications (e.g. PMI, PRINCE2) to compliment your program management experience
Asian market experience
Travel industry / e-commerce / tech / consulting experience

Introduction:

ICES is currently seeking an Information Management Analyst to join our Data Quality & Information Management Department. Reporting to the Lead Specialist, the Information Management Analyst is responsible for the import and maintenance of large health services data sets in a SAS/LINUX environment under stringent confidentiality and security guidelines. The Information Management Analyst will convert the administrative data to SAS datasets, perform data cleaning and validation activities, document data characteristics, and perform routine data archiving activities and implementation of ICES data destruction policy. The Information Management Analyst will assume data management and processing responsibilities of ICES record linkage research projects. The Information Management Analyst will demonstrate a comprehensive understanding of specific ICES data holdings and ICES’ privacy, confidentiality and security policies and Guidelines.

Responsibilities of the position include, but may not be limited to:

Recode any direct personal identifiers as it arrives at ICES as the first use;
Develop and process SAS programs to convert administrative and study data files to SAS datasets;
Act as an ICES Administrative Data Covenanter;
Perform data cleaning and validation activities, documentation of data characteristics according to P&B standards and guidelines;
Perform electronic archiving of specific ICES databases;
Carry out data destruction following ICES data destruction policy;
Receive data collected in ICES primary data collection projects and prepares for the ICES research environment (LINUX);
Perform ad-hoc data transferring requests;
Communicate with Technology department, Research Program Managers, and/or Project Managers to solve data issues;
Communicate with ICES data providers as necessary;
Other duties as may be assigned within the scope of this position.

Knowledge, skills, and abilities required: 
Bachelor’s degree in computer science, Biostatistics, or related field;
3 years of related work experience;
Working knowledge of principles of computer systems architecture, database design and record linkage methodology;
Proficient in SAS programming;
Excellent understanding of the concepts of data privacy, confidentiality, and security practices;
Understanding of the LINUX operating system for data security management practices, ICES Primary Data Collection Utility and how to use administrative data in health services research is an asset;
Beginner to intermediate proficiency in other programming languages like SQL and python would be an advantage;
Good organizational skills;
Excellent oral and written communication skills.
 
This is a full-time opportunity at ICES Central. Successful candidate must reside within Ontario while working remotely and able to come into the office if required from time to time. There may be instances where in-person meetings are requested; however, ICES continues to support Flexible remote work arrangements anywhere in Ontario.

Security clearance may be required.

Interested candidates should submit their resume and cover letter detailing how their knowledge, skills and abilities match the scope of this position.

We thank all applicants for their interest in working at ICES. Due to the volume of applications received, only applicants being considered for the position will be contacted for further discussions.

Company Description

Make an impact at a global and dynamic investment organization

When you invest your career in CPP Investments, you join one of the most respected and fastest growing institutional investors in the world. With current assets under management valued in excess of $500 billion, CPP Investments is a professional investment management organization that globally invests the funds of the Canada Pension Plan (CPP) to help ensure long-term sustainability. The CPP Fund is projected to reach $3 trillion by 2050. CPP Investments invests in all major asset classes, including public equity, private equity, real estate, infrastructure and fixed-income instruments, and is headquartered in Toronto with offices in Hong Kong, London, Luxembourg, Mumbai, New York City, San Francisco, São Paulo and Sydney.

Job Description

The Business Intelligence team is responsible for delivering Total Fund reporting and analytics to consumers across the organization. The team works directly with Total Fund Management, Performance and Technology & Data collaboratively to establish processes, procedures, systems, and controls to ensure the accuracy and completeness of the quality of our enriched portfolio dataset.

Reporting into the Manager, Business Intelligence, the Senior Analyst will use their strong technical capabilities to support the daily Total Fund reporting process critical to investment decision-making, trade execution, servicing and reporting.

Role-Specific Accountabilities

Support the timely and accurate publishing of total fund level reporting, including performing analysis to identify and explain significant changes to the Total Fund asset and exposure composition.
Leveraging technical tools (i.e. SQL, Python, Excel macros), perform complex data analysis on large volumes of unstructured data to investigate and resolve reporting exceptions.
Proactively identify opportunities to improve Total Fund reporting and processes through automation or process enhancements; lead the implementation of the enhancements internally and/ or through cross functional collaboration.
Actively support partnerships with Enterprise Data Management and Technology in continuously enhance portfolio data quality & delivery and self-serve reporting capabilities (e.g. data visualization, Tableau) based on end user requirements.
Work with Investment Departments and Operations teams to identify evolving reporting needs to support investment decision-making. Assist in gathering business requirements, coordination the user acceptance testing and provide ongoing training to downstream users. 

Qualifications

2+ years of finance industry work experience
Strong programing skills in Python, SQL, and Excel/VBA
Strong knowledge of financial products and derivative instruments
Undergraduate degree in relevant field (Computer Science, Math, Engineering) is an asset
Ability to work independently and is a self-starter
Demonstrated a thirst for learning new concepts and skills in a fast-paced, team-oriented environment
Demonstrated ability to meet deadlines and work under pressure
Strong communication and interpersonal skills
Exemplifies our Guiding Principles of integrity, partnership, and high performance

About the job
Role Overview

The Data Science & Analytics team is expanding within Consumer Marketing organization, with a laser focus on building data tools, supporting experimentation, develop predictive models and extract data-driven insights to achieve our goals for a direct-to-consumer marketing organization which supports 400 million customers worldwide. With a focus on our Retention business, this is an opportunity to work with creative businesspeople who are change agents for our business practices and methodologies and affecting top-line revenue. This is a high-visibility role working with Retention Marketing, sales, finance, and senior business leaders.

This is a remote role based in the US or Canada. We are only considering candidates located in the US or Canada and are not offering relocation at this time.

More About The Role

As a Senior Business Data Analyst, using your analytical and programming background together with your problem-solving skills, you will help extract the secrets of our data, translating data findings into customer insights. You will do so by discovering and transforming the data, performing ad-hoc data analysis, and developing data tools and dashboards for the Marketing Retention team to allow them to monitor the essential metrics to identify pain points and improve business outcomes. You are curious about data, passionate about telling stories based on data, and willing to be data experts of reference within the organization.

Work with Retention Marketing specialists to form creative solutions and design experiments using deep statistical knowledge to guide marketing insights.
Solve ad-hoc data questions from the Marketing Retention team.
Run data analysis to support experimentation and convert analytical findings into customer insights that power marketing strategies and programs across end-to-end customer journey.
Design, develop, and automate data tools and dashboards that allow monitoring metrics in a highly scalable self-service way.
Implement data hygiene, data standardization, and data transformation that optimizes other data processes. 
Partner with different team members to solve data problems, identify trends, and find opportunities. 

About You

You have 5+ years of progressive experience in a data analyst role including data mining, data transformation, and delivering relevant insights.
You have 3+ years of experience in programming with SQL, Python, or R for exploring and transforming data within a relational database environment.
You have 3+ years of experience in data visualization tools such as Tableau, Power BI, R Shiny, D3.js, etc.
You have 2+ years of experience in Statistical Testing (Frequentist A/B testing, Bayesian A/B testing, or Multivariate testing) and design of experiments.
Passion for working in a marketing team of a B2C product and for applying data analytics to improve business results.
Professional experience in hypothesis testing, design of experiments, data mining, data visualization, and data manipulation/transformation.
Experience in handling large datasets in big data environments using Py Spark is a bonus.
Experience working in Databricks within a cloud environment (Azure, AWS) is a bonus.
Experience with MicroStrategy, Adobe Analytics, or Google Analytics.

About the job
Summary of Duties:
Reporting to the Corporate Information Officer, the Database Administrator and Data Governance Analyst (DBA) is responsible for the maintenance, security, and efficient operation of both Oracle and SQL servers and databases. This role oversees the City's data policies, ensuring data security and governance. The DBA is involved in applying updates, generating reports, assisting with data conversions for upcoming projects, and maintaining all application databases.
This position works with the various members of the Information Technology team to create efficiencies, review current processes, analyze, and develop or modify databases including coding stored procedures, testing, debugging, and installing database software. This position provides direction and guidance on the use of the various technologies for process improvements usability and accessibility.
 Duties and Responsibilities:
(These set out the principal functions of the position, and shall not be considered as a detailed description of all the work requirements).
Develop databases for new applications which includes building development, testing, user acceptance and production databases.
Develop standards for database structures. Write technical procedures and documentation for database technology including operations, user guide, etc.
Develop database backup and recovery scripts for new databases and database environments including disaster recovery procedures.
Optimize database structures for application performance. Monitor database environment's disk & CPU usage. Ensure environments has sufficient resources.

About The Role

CrowdStrike Intelligence, a core component of CrowdStrike Counter Adversary Operations, is seeking a Senior Intelligence Analyst for its Global Threat Analysis Cell (GTAC) to focus on targeted intrusion activity related to China-nexus adversaries. This position will be primarily focused on tracking known adversaries and other cyber operations believed to emanate from China, as well as identifying and tracking trends associated with these operations. The Senior Intelligence Analyst will be required to research and report on cyber operations at both the strategic and tactical level as part of a close-knit team where collaboration is a critical driver for mission success. This position is instrumental in providing unique insight into adversary operations through finished Intelligence products used by CrowdStrike customers and stakeholders.

What You'll Do

Proactively identify and track targeted intrusion cyber threats, trends, and new developments by China-nexus adversaries through analysis of raw intelligence and data 
Apply analytic best practices and tradecraft to gathered intelligence in a consistent manner
Provide finished intelligence analysis and assessments to internal and external customers through written reporting, in varying predetermined suspense and depth, with minimal supervision
Collaborate across teams to inform various functions within CrowdStrike Intelligence about activity of interest and to coordinate adversary/campaign tracking, as well as enrich finished intelligence products
Identify intelligence gaps and submit requests for information to fill gaps
Provide peer review of proposed/draft reporting and analytic uplift to team members 
Prioritize, categorize, and respond to requests for information from internal and external customers
Conduct briefings as needed for a variety of levels of customers as requested (via either phone, video conference, webcast, in-person briefing, or industry conference)

What You'll Need

Motivated self-starter with 5+ years’ experience in a threat intelligence and cybersecurity environment, with a focus on state-nexus cyber operations
Comprehensive, practical knowledge of research/collection tradecraft and analytical methods—to include intrusion analysis
Strong analytic writing skills, particularly the ability to produce quality finished intelligence products on short deadlines as well as continuing to maintain analysis for, and report on, long-term strategic assessments with minimal assistance
Familiarity with computer networking fundamentals, computer network defense (CND) operations, host-based forensics and network traffic monitoring
Ability to independently identify and track adversary tradecraft trends 
Understanding of technical terminology, tools, and tactics employed by threat actors
An enthusiasm for collaboration, including being comfortable working in a team-oriented environment as well as across multiple teams to leverage subject matter expertise of colleagues
Passionate about taking the initiative to identify and develop new visibility into adversary operations
Ability or willingness to learn to conduct technical analysis of the tools and tradecraft used by threat actors
Knowledge of geopolitical issues and ability to use that information to support understanding of current and future impacts on the cyber threat landscape
Undergraduate degree, military training or relevant experience in cyber intelligence, computer science, general intelligence studies, security studies, political science, international relations, etc. 
Other technical security certifications or academic background, such as a graduate degree, are a plus.

VTS is the commercial real estate industry’s only technology company that unifies owners, operators, brokers, and tenants in a single platform to capitalize on opportunities revealed in every square foot of their properties. In 2013, VTS revolutionized the commercial real estate industry’s leasing operations with what is now VTS Lease. Field Competitive Intelligence Analyst, Americas (Remote CT/MT) 

About The Role

As a Field Competitive Intelligence Analyst, you will support the CrowdStrike Sales and Executive Teams. You will work and support the CTO Labs and Field CTO Teams team at CrowdStrike. The Field CI team’s mission is to identify & deliver key competitive differentiators to support the international growth of customers, new markets, and TAM. This includes driving strategy through cross functional collaboration across the company including Product, Sales, Marketing, and more.

As the Field CI Analyst, you will be responsible for creating and communicating the company’s competitive differentiation strategy on a regional basis and working closely with the company’s product CTO’s, Product Managers and Field functions on a regular basis. You will also work closely with other groups within CrowdStrike, which includes: marketing, value management, legal and corporate affairs teams.

This role reports to the Manager, Competitive Intelligence Strategy. With your extensive cybersecurity background and your ability to think and operate at a strategic level, you will drive CrowdStrike’s technical vision and strategy and support on strategic engagements across the CrowdStrike organization.

What You'll Do

Support current customers and new customers by sharing CrowdStrike’s key competitive value differentiators, supporting the positioning of CrowdStrike as the leading thought leader for Cybersecurity with customers, partners, and analysts.
Driving and communicating CrowdStrike’s technology strategy to customers and partners as well as industry events.
Maintaining an in-depth knowledge of the cyber security industry, the competitive landscape and related industry developments to ensure we continue to be thought leaders who innovate ahead of the market.
Using stakeholders’ feedback to inform necessary improvements and adjustments to technology.
Focusing on technology improvements that will improve competitive positioning of the CrowdStrike products.
Providing recommendations for continuous improvement.

What You'll Need

Deep technical and operations skills in understanding the capabilities (strengths and weaknesses) of competitor offerings.
Strong analytical and communication skills to allow translation of competitive differentiation points into contextually relevant talking points.
Demonstrate a deep and broad knowledge of security issues and trends and are able to articulate a high-level security strategy to both technical and non-technical audiences.
Working in a role such as or similar to Competitive Strategist, Strategic Consultant, Enterprise Security Architect.
Experience with/exposure to Endpoint Security, Cloud Security, SIEM/Log Management, Mobile Security, Identity Security, Incident Response as well as other cyber security domains.
Regional travel is expected on a limited basis.

About The Role

CrowdStrike Intelligence, a core component of CrowdStrike Counter Adversary Operations, is seeking a Senior Intelligence Analyst for its Global Threat Analysis Cell (GTAC) to focus on targeted intrusion activity related to China-nexus adversaries. This position will be primarily focused on tracking known adversaries and other cyber operations believed to emanate from China, as well as identifying and tracking trends associated with these operations. The Senior Intelligence Analyst will be required to research and report on cyber operations at both the strategic and tactical level as part of a close-knit team where collaboration is a critical driver for mission success. This position is instrumental in providing unique insight into adversary operations through finished Intelligence products used by CrowdStrike customers and stakeholders.

What You'll Do

Proactively identify and track targeted intrusion cyber threats, trends, and new developments by China-nexus adversaries through analysis of raw intelligence and data 
Apply analytic best practices and tradecraft to gathered intelligence in a consistent manner
Provide finished intelligence analysis and assessments to internal and external customers through written reporting, in varying predetermined suspense and depth, with minimal supervision
Collaborate across teams to inform various functions within CrowdStrike Intelligence about activity of interest and to coordinate adversary/campaign tracking, as well as enrich finished intelligence products
Identify intelligence gaps and submit requests for information to fill gaps
Provide peer review of proposed/draft reporting and analytic uplift to team members 
Prioritize, categorize, and respond to requests for information from internal and external customers
Conduct briefings as needed for a variety of levels of customers as requested (via either phone, video conference, webcast, in-person briefing, or industry conference)

What You'll Need

Motivated self-starter with 5+ years’ experience in a threat intelligence and cybersecurity environment, with a focus on state-nexus cyber operations
Comprehensive, practical knowledge of research/collection tradecraft and analytical methods—to include intrusion analysis
Strong analytic writing skills, particularly the ability to produce quality finished intelligence products on short deadlines as well as continuing to maintain analysis for, and report on, long-term strategic assessments with minimal assistance
Familiarity with computer networking fundamentals, computer network defense (CND) operations, host-based forensics and network traffic monitoring
Ability to independently identify and track adversary tradecraft trends 
Understanding of technical terminology, tools, and tactics employed by threat actors
An enthusiasm for collaboration, including being comfortable working in a team-oriented environment as well as across multiple teams to leverage subject matter expertise of colleagues
Passionate about taking the initiative to identify and develop new visibility into adversary operations
Ability or willingness to learn to conduct technical analysis of the tools and tradecraft used by threat actors
Knowledge of geopolitical issues and ability to use that information to support understanding of current and future impacts on the cyber threat landscape
Undergraduate degree, military training or relevant experience in cyber intelligence, computer science, general intelligence studies, security studies, political science, international relations, etc. 
Other technical security certifications or academic background, such as a graduate degree, are a plus.

Automate manual operational processes and present back on time savings gained through modernization of business operations

What you’ll Need to Succeed:

Bachelor’s degree or higher in Mathematics, Business, Economics, Data Science, Information Technology or similar field
Bachelor’s Degree or higher in computer sciences, engineering, mathematics, statistics, data science or a related degree program. Masters degree preferred
Advanced domain of data analysis and data visualization tools and software such as Excel, SQL, Tableau, Python or similar
Analytical mindset, with proven track record in using data to measure performance and make decisions
Excellent problem-solving skills including the ability to analyze and resolve complex problems using data
Ability to work under pressure in a fast-paced and rapidly changing environment
Excellent communication skills (both verbal and written), with proven ability to convey complex messages clearly and with conviction
Team player with strong interpersonal, relationship-building, and stakeholder management skills

Job Description

Who We Are

BGIS is a leading provider of customized facility management and real estate services. With our combined team of over 6,500 globally, we relentlessly focus on enabling innovation through the services we deliver, while actively looking for new opportunities that will enable innovation for our clients’ businesses. Globally, we manage over 320 million square feet of client portfolios across 30,000+ locations in North America, Europe, Middle East, Australia and Asia. Further information is available at www.bgis.com

Summary

The Fleet Analyst and Logistics Coordinator (FALC) works as an integral member of the back-office team supporting Regional Operations Managers, BGIS ITS Technicians, and senior executives by analyzing the daily operations and maintenance activities necessary for safe, reliable, and efficient operations. They are responsible for keeping all Fleet data files up to date, supporting the planning, scheduling, and analysis of preventative and corrective maintenance activities.

The FALC is a supporting role who will work with the branch contacts to coordinate necessary fleet changes, repairs, GPS installations, maintenance visits, and any training. The FALC is expected to execute this work according to BGIS standard practices and is responsible to effectively maintain an up- to –date fleet list. The FALC is also responsible for supporting in the financial management of the data of the daily vehicle GPS logs, and fleet costs.

Key Duties & Responsibilities

Team Member Support

Acts as a liaison between the Corporate Fleet team and the individual branch managers to drive efficiencies in fleet activities. 
Tracks and follows up with all vehicle maintenance logs and inspection records to ensure accurate and up to date file systems.
Assists local branch support with transfer of vehicles between locations, scheduling repairs and maintenance. 
Meets with various leadership to review any trends in mismatched timecard to GPS data.
Determines and coordinates the distribution of assets based upon provided criteria. 


Reporting and Analysis

Completes high volume file management; ensuring files are complete, accurate, and continually updated.
Maintains weekly GPS extract to compare against the individual technician’s timesheets.
Manages cost reporting by vehicle to ensure real-time data on maintenance, lease, repair costs for the lifetime of the vehicle.
Supports the Regional Managers in scheduling repairs & replacements to ensure the least amount of down time per technician. 


 Inventory Forecast Support

Works with leadership and Corporate Fleet to forecast the purchase of replacement assets in order to maintain accurate inventory levels by location.


Dashboard Development Support

Collaborates with the Strategic Team to develop dashboards for accurate reporting leading in order to drive cost efficiencies. 
Other duties as assigned.


Knowledge & Skills

Business Diploma or Degree, relevant work experience is an asset. 
Display excellent interpersonal and communication skills, both written and verbal is essential.
Ability to pay strong attention to detail.
Ability to multitask, prioritize, stay organized, and perform in a deadline-oriented environment.
Analyze problems and have problem-solving skills.
Work independently as well as in a team-based environment.
Work in a fast-paced environment.
Display strong knowledge of relevant computer applications.
General knowledge of corporate automobile’s considered an asset. 
Strong organizational, coordination and documentation skills with the ability to multi-task.
Proficient with MS Office, specifically advanced Excel skills.


Licenses and/or Professional Accreditation

Valid driver’s license.

Introduction

A career in IBM Consulting is rooted by long-term relationships and close collaboration with clients across the globe.

You'll work with visionaries across multiple industries to improve the hybrid cloud and AI journey for the most innovative and valuable companies in the world. Your ability to accelerate impact and make meaningful change for your clients is enabled by our strategic partner ecosystem and our robust technology platforms across the IBM portfolio; including Software and Red Hat.

Curiosity and a constant quest for knowledge serve as the foundation to success in IBM Consulting. In your role, you'll be encouraged to challenge the norm, investigate ideas outside of your role, and come up with creative solutions resulting in ground breaking impact for a wide network of clients. Our culture of evolution and empathy centers on long-term career growth and development opportunities in an environment that embraces your unique skills and experience.

Your Role and Responsibilities

As a SAP Consultant you will serve as a client-facing practitioner who sells, leads and implements expert services utilizing the breadth of IBM's offerings and technologies. A successful SAP Consultant is regarded by clients as a trusted business advisor who collaborates to provide innovative solutions used to solve the most challenging business problems.

You will work on projects that help clients integrate strategy, process, technology, and information to increase effectiveness, reduce costs and improve profit and shareholder value. You can take advantage of opportunities to master new skills, work across different disciplines, move into new challenges and develop a robust understanding of different industries.

As SAP Analytics consultant, you will deliver innovative analytical/reporting solutions utilizing the most current versions of SAP solutions to ensure successful SAP implementations by collaborating with cross functional business and technical resources.

This position requires excellent verbal and written communication skills, ability to interact with both business and technical stakeholders of client companies and a proven track record designing and implementing S/4 HANA embedded analytics, SAP HANA Cloud Solutions, SAP Datasphere & SAP Analytics Cloud (SAC). You will be a team player, proactive, an effective communicator with ability to work independently.

Required Technical and Professional Expertise


5+ years’ experience in implementing SAP Analytical/Reporting for various industry sectors
Technical understanding of one or more SAP software tools for analytics such as SAP Datasphere, SAP S/4 HANA Embedded Analytcis, SAP Analytics Cloud, SAP HANA Cloud.
Experience in the remediation of SAP BWonHANA or SAP BW/4 HANA when ECC is migrated to S/4 HANA.
Develop functional/technical specification documents and design technical solution to support analytical/reporting deliverables
Participated in all the aspects of the project life cycle; including gathering requirements, Gap Analysis and blueprinting, system configuration, customization, testing, documenting, deployment and training end-users
min. 2 full cycle implementations of SAP S/4 HANA Embedded Analytics and minimum one implementation of SAP Datasphere, SAP Analytics Cloud and SAP HANA Cloud in production environment

About you and this role - What you will do in this role

Monitors production deviation from standard, investigates the root cause for the deviation and corrects production and inventory data in SAP, as appropriate. Reconciles and closes production/period orders after all production posting is complete, monitors and balances inventories and performs routine month end close activities. Requires full proficiency in a range of technical, operational, or analytical/scientific processes and procedures through job-related training and considerable on the job experience to perform a variety of work assignments. Acts as an informal resource for team members with less experience.

Responsibilities - Duties, projects, tasks, and activities you would be responsible for in this role

Production Data Analyst/Raw Material Coordinator:

Analyze each production order to ensure proper raw material allocation 
Determine if all posting against production order is complete
Monitor cost variance and utility yield data in SAP at an appropriate frequency and identify items that are exceeding the deviation tolerance as documented in the Business rules for each production order
Make adjustments to data in SAP as required following the Business rules (timeliness and accuracy)
Investigate the cause for deviation to identify if a posting error or a process change has occurred
Lead root cause analysis for posting errors and develop action plan to eliminate the root cause
Perform SAP transaction to make appropriate production posting corrections
Ensure all month end physical inventory counts of raw materials are taken in a timely manner
Compile inventories of all raw materials at month end
Reconcile raw material and product inventory discrepancies and makes necessary adjustments to correct inventories
Investigate large variances between SAP inventories and audited inventories to identify if a posting error or a process error has occurred
File Certificates of Analysis (COAs) 
Complete inventory adjustments and month end close reports by the globally accepted time required
Collect data for yearly Green House Gas Emissions report 
Enters SAP transactions for receiving raw materials 
Manages raw material inventory counts (weekly/monthly) 
Creates Purchase Orders for LP7 (raw materials, capital & expense, yearly PO’s) 
Order necessary process materials and chemicals for LP7 Operations 
Track Hexene and Isopentane rail cars. Enter new cars into the plants tracking system
Review production schedule on a weekly basis to determine raw material inventories match future production requirements 
Verify accounting invoices and respond to Accounting questions of the raw materials when required
Improvements to traceability of Raw materials.   Long term work within Quality Systems to further develop documentation and maintain raw material traceability
Confirm on a weekly basis nitrogen supply versus billing from Praxair 
Arrange shipping documents for empty TEAL, TnHAL, catalyst cylinders, totes 
Liaise with Warehouse Personnel and Yard Master 
Provide forecast/details of Hydrogen usage

Introduction

A career in IBM Consulting is rooted by long-term relationships and close collaboration with clients across the globe.

You'll work with visionaries across multiple industries to improve the hybrid cloud and AI journey for the most innovative and valuable companies in the world. Your ability to accelerate impact and make meaningful change for your clients is enabled by our strategic partner ecosystem and our robust technology platforms across the IBM portfolio; including Software and Red Hat.

Curiosity and a constant quest for knowledge serve as the foundation to success in IBM Consulting. In your role, you'll be encouraged to challenge the norm, investigate ideas outside of your role, and come up with creative solutions resulting in ground breaking impact for a wide network of clients. Our culture of evolution and empathy centers on long-term career growth and development opportunities in an environment that embraces your unique skills and experience.

Your Role and Responsibilities

As a SAP Consultant you will serve as a client-facing practitioner who sells, leads and implements expert services utilizing the breadth of IBM's offerings and technologies. A successful SAP Consultant is regarded by clients as a trusted business advisor who collaborates to provide innovative solutions used to solve the most challenging business problems.

You will work on projects that help clients integrate strategy, process, technology, and information to increase effectiveness, reduce costs and improve profit and shareholder value. You can take advantage of opportunities to master new skills, work across different disciplines, move into new challenges and develop a robust understanding of different industries.

As SAP Analytics consultant, you will deliver innovative analytical/reporting solutions utilizing the most current versions of SAP solutions to ensure successful SAP implementations by collaborating with cross functional business and technical resources.

This position requires excellent verbal and written communication skills, ability to interact with both business and technical stakeholders of client companies and a proven track record designing and implementing S/4 HANA embedded analytics, SAP HANA Cloud Solutions, SAP Datasphere & SAP Analytics Cloud (SAC). You will be a team player, proactive, an effective communicator with ability to work independently.

Required Technical and Professional Expertise


5+ years’ experience in implementing SAP Analytical/Reporting for various industry sectors
Technical understanding of one or more SAP software tools for analytics such as SAP Datasphere, SAP S/4 HANA Embedded Analytcis, SAP Analytics Cloud, SAP HANA Cloud.
Experience in the remediation of SAP BWonHANA or SAP BW/4 HANA when ECC is migrated to S/4 HANA.
Develop functional/technical specification documents and design technical solution to support analytical/reporting deliverables
Participated in all the aspects of the project life cycle; including gathering requirements, Gap Analysis and blueprinting, system configuration, customization, testing, documenting, deployment and training end-users
min. 2 full cycle implementations of SAP S/4 HANA Embedded Analytics and minimum one implementation of SAP Datasphere, SAP Analytics Cloud and SAP HANA Cloud in production environment
Experience with data acquisition tools (BODS, SLT, SDI, ODQ/ODP, CDS, Cloud Connectors...)
Working knowledge of SAP implementation activities from an Activate perspective, Prepare, Explore, Realize Build, Realize Test, Deploy and Support to Sustainment.

Reporting to the Project Manager, the Business Analyst III, Data Governance is responsible for establishing and maintaining Seaspan Marine Group’s information and data governance processes within our data and digital environments. In addition to creating the standards and supporting usage consistency across our information and data assets, this role will actively work with stakeholders to ensure business alignment, generate awareness on information and data governance principles, drive their implementation, and provide support for their adoption.

Note: This position qualifies for an optional hybrid work schedule after 90 days of onsite work and onboarding. Employee will be subject to the terms of the Flexible Work Policy Agreement.

What You’ll Do
Informational and Data Governance Framework:
Defines and establishes a comprehensive governance framework encompassing standards, policies, and key processes associated with Seaspan Marine Group’s informational and data environments, such as Azure, SharePoint sites and pages, Power BI workspaces, Power App workspaces, etc.
Develop and implement governance policies and procedures across the business.
Regularly updates policies to reflect changes in our organizational landscape and evolving industry standards.
Oversees and implements metadata management, information and data classification, and categorization across the different digital and data platforms to enhance data organization and accessibility.
Ensures alignment with internal and external requirements for an accurate and secure management of our information and data assets throughout their lifecycle.

Stakeholder Engagement And Collaboration
Collaborates with business and technical stakeholders to understand their current information and data needs, as well their future challenges.
Collects and document requirements, leveraging use cases that can be replicated across departments and platforms.
Facilitates the communication and awareness of governance expectations among department heads, while ensuring adherence to agreed processes and assigned roles.
Conducts training sessions to inform stakeholders on data governance processes and principles.
Provides strategic guidance on data-related governance best practices.
Supports the implementation of the Data and Digital Enablement Program’s roadmap.
Participates in Scrum ceremonies as part of the Data and Digital Enablement team.

Business Data Stewardship
Establishes and maintains business data stewardship processes to promote accountability and responsibility for data quality and compliance.
Monitors and evaluates data governance effectiveness, identifying opportunities for improvement and driving necessary changes.

Experience with business process redesign, including development of as-is and to-be states.

What You’ll Be Doing

CIBC Asset Management (CIBC AM) is one of Canada's largest asset management firms with approximately $180 billion in assets under management and possess over forty-five years of experience designing and implementing client solutions. We are leaders in providing a broad range of high-quality global investment management solutions to retail and institutional clients.

Our assets include those under institutional money management for pension funds, endowments and insurance funds, private wealth management, and those that are part of the CIBC family of mutual funds.

At CIBC, our goal is to help our clients achieve what matters to them. Our philosophy is based on the CIBC values of Trust, Teamwork, and Accountability and we achieve results for our clients through an in-depth disciplined investing approach based on rigor and research.

As Quantitative Analyst, you will apply your knowledge and experience of data modelling to solve challenging business problems and bring innovative solutions. This role is focused on the development and interpretation of practical quantitative strategies to be used as part of our Multi-Asset and Currency investment processes.

The Multi-Asset and Currency Investment group is a Montreal based team with assets north of $40B. You will be responsible for maintaining and improving models that predict relative or absolute returns in country, currencies, equities, global fixed income, and alternative asset classes including commodities and volatility. You’ll work with structured and unstructured datasets taking models from experiment to deployment in the form of tools, strategies and portfolios. You will contribute to the process of finding, cleaning, storing and accessing data related to global financial markets.

At CIBC we enable the work environment most optimal for you to thrive in your role. Details on your work arrangement (proportion of on-site and remote work) will be discussed at the time of your interview.

How You’ll Succeed

Quantitative Research. You will apply new and well established techniques to the problem of creating portfolios which add value for clients whilst controlling risk. You will draw on academic sources, industry research and insights from team members for new ideas to test. Research may include finding signals that help predict asset returns, applying new algorithms to our established factors, testing new portfolio construction algorithms and assessing the risk environment
Communication. You will have good interpersonal, verbal and written communication skills. Able to explain concisely highly technical information to audiences with varying technical expertise. You will have the ability to constructively challenge model methodologies, assumptions and validation approach.
Programming. You will write and run programs in Python. You will create functions, classes, modules or similar tools that other members of the quantitative research team can use. You will contribute to the on-going development of our back-testing, portfolio construction and risk architecture.
Problem solving and Critical thinking. You will be able to accurately identify a problem’s source, severity, and impact to determine possible solutions and required resources.

Who You Are

You can demonstrate advanced knowledge and deep understanding of asset class, factor and portfolio modeling obtained through 4-7 years of practical experience.
You have extensive hands-on experience in Python and a proven ability to quickly learn and adapt to new tools. 
You love to learn and share your learning. You're passionate about growing your knowledge, and sharing your knowledge.
You understand that success is in the details. You notice things that others don't. Your critical thinking skills help to inform your decision making.

About the job
Why join us?

Are you looking to join an innovative, global real estate company who builds communities and connects people to exceptional places? If so, we would love to tell you our story.

At Oxford, our culture is truly one of a kind. Across business lines and around the world, we embrace the complex and tackle opportunities with speed and agility. We are ambitious and humble, forward looking and service-focused. We get stuff done, and have fun doing it! We take great pride in contributing to the communities where we live. We believe that what is good for the environment is good for business. Together we deliver exceptional experiences to our over 2 million daily customers.

Oxford is seeking a Technical Analyst to join our Valuations & Analytics team in Toronto, Canada. Oxford’s Valuations & Analytics team is responsible for real estate valuations, portfolio and property performance and risk analysis across all markets that Oxford invests. The ideal candidate will combine solid technical skills with a desire to learn real estate finance as an integral part of the Valuations & Analytics team. The candidate for this position will be exposed to the valuation and asset management analytics of investment properties across Oxford’s global portfolio.

As a member of this team, you will be responsible for 

Designing, building and maintaining reports, tools and templates used to create and maintain Oxford valuation models using VBA, SQL and / or related skills;
Assist in the development and maintenance of the team’s database, which tracks historic and forecast property results and market information;
Liaise with Oxford’s Information Technology team as well as third party systems service providers in the sourcing, development and maintenance of internally and externally managed software and systems;
Lead regular testing and implementation of annual system upgrades and process improvements;
Conduct market and economic research, assemble and interpret macro-market trends.
Participate in the creation and maintenance of valuation models primarily using Argus Enterprise to reflect changes to the portfolio and market conditions; 
Liaise with accountants, asset managers, leasing and property management groups in data collection for periodic valuation updates; and
Prepare annual written valuation reports.

To succeed in this role, you have 

Relevant undergraduate or advanced degree with 1-4 years of work experience;
Candidates must have completed some computer programming courses at a post-secondary level and have a well-developed understanding of the principles of programming;
Proficiency in SQL, VBA (or equivalents), and Microsoft Excel (financial modeling) is required;
Knowledge and experience with data visualization or business intelligence software is considered an asset;
Demonstrated interest in, or prior work experience, in real estate or investment finance is considered an asset;
Knowledge and experience with ARGUS Enterprise is considered an asset;
Self-motivated individual with a strong work ethic and a high level of attention to detail;
Strong verbal and written communication, interpersonal, problem solving and project management skills;
Ability to work well under pressure with multiple competing deadlines;
Flexible attitude towards a variety of work tasks is required;
Valid Passport for International travel as needed.

Our story

Oxford Properties Group (“Oxford”) is a leading global real estate investor, asset manager and business builder. It builds, buys, and grows defined real estate operating business with world-class management teams. Established in 1960, Oxford and its portfolio companies manage approximately C$87 billion of assets across four continents on behalf of their investment partners. Oxford’s owned portfolio encompasses office, logistics, retail, multifamily residential, life sciences, hotels, alternatives and credit in global gateway cities and high-growth hubs. A thematic investor with a committed source of capital, Oxford invests in properties, portfolios, development sites, debt, securities, and real estate businesses across the risk-reward spectrum. Together with its portfolio companies, Oxford is one of the world’s most active developers with over 80 projects currently underway globally across all major asset classes. Oxford is owned by OMERS, the Canadian defined benefit pension plan for Ontario's municipal employees.

For more information on Oxford, visit www.oxfordproperties.com

OMERS is committed to having a workforce that reflects the communities in which we live and work. We are an equal opportunity employer committed to a barrier-free recruitment and selection process. At OMERS inclusion and diversity means belonging. How we create a sense of belonging is through our employees and our vast network of Employee Resource Groups. Whether you are passionate about gender, pride, or visible minorities, we have groups that are focused on making a difference in all of our lives.

About the job
Why Mozilla?

Mozilla Corporation is the non-profit-backed technology company that has shaped the internet for the better over the last 25 years. We make pioneering brands like Firefox, the privacy-minded web browser, and Pocket, a service for keeping up with the best content online. Now, with more than 225 million people around the world using our products each month, we’re shaping the next 25 years of technology and helping to reclaim an internet built for people, not companies. Our work focuses on diverse areas including AI, social media, security and more. And we’re doing this while never losing our focus on our core mission – to make the internet better for people.

The Mozilla Corporation is wholly owned by the non-profit 501(c) Mozilla Foundation. This means we aren’t beholden to any shareholders — only to our mission. Along with 60,000+ volunteer contributors and collaborators all over the world, Mozillians design, build and distribute open-source software that enables people to enjoy the internet on their terms.

About This Team And Role

In this role, you will sit at the cross section of Media Activations, Product Marketing, Web and Data Science, collaborating with these teams to define business impact, build capabilities and analyze data that helps shape future business growth. You’ll also be a key client contact to the media agency of record, ensuring that agency output is aligned with our business strategy.

Responsibilities

Analyze marketing campaigns and customer data to assess their effectiveness and ROI.
Provide actionable insights to enhance marketing strategies and optimize budgets.
Partner with Data Science to build the roadmap for marketing attribution needs across the portfolio
Work with teams across Marketing to streamline our data sources, analyze results and outline how results impact business outcomes
Build a working model between Marketing and Data Science, connecting the dots between Marketing data and Product data
Work with media agency Analytics team to deliver reporting that fits Mozilla’s business needs
Analytics thought leadership (full funnel coordination, marketplace changes, new ad technology)
Building and implementing measurement plans (KPIs across funnel/media channels that creates overall storytelling around campaign success)

Requirements

Bachelor's degree in Business, Statistics, Economics, or a related quantitative field.
Minimum 10 years of proven experience in marketing analytics at a media agency or client side/industry.
Proficiency in statistical analysis and data visualization tools (e.g., Python, R, Tableau).
Proficiency in marketing analytics tools (e.g., Google Analytics, Adobe Analytics).
Strong analytical and problem-solving skills; translate data and insights into actions and recommendations, communicating in a concise, honest, and understandable way.
Deep knowledge of the advertising landscape and ability to translate that knowledge for Mozilla’s unique business needs.
Comfortable leading and collaborating in a constantly evolving marketing environment.
Experience running and analyzing A/B tests.
Excellent quantitative and qualitative skills, you are able to break down highly complex problems involving large amounts of data.
Strong storytelling skills and ability to tailor data and insights to different audiences.
Strong project management capabilities and ability to drive multiple work streams of varying complexity.

Introduction

A career in IBM Consulting is rooted by long-term relationships and close collaboration with clients across the globe.

You'll work with visionaries across multiple industries to improve the hybrid cloud and AI journey for the most innovative and valuable companies in the world. Your ability to accelerate impact and make meaningful change for your clients is enabled by our strategic partner ecosystem and our robust technology platforms across the IBM portfolio; including Software and Red Hat.

Curiosity and a constant quest for knowledge serve as the foundation to success in IBM Consulting. In your role, you'll be encouraged to challenge the norm, investigate ideas outside of your role, and come up with creative solutions resulting in ground breaking impact for a wide network of clients. Our culture of evolution and empathy centers on long-term career growth and development opportunities in an environment that embraces your unique skills and experience.

Your Role and Responsibilities

As a SAP Consultant you will serve as a client-facing practitioner who sells, leads and implements expert services utilizing the breadth of IBM's offerings and technologies. A successful SAP Consultant is regarded by clients as a trusted business advisor who collaborates to provide innovative solutions used to solve the most challenging business problems.

You will work on projects that help clients integrate strategy, process, technology, and information to increase effectiveness, reduce costs and improve profit and shareholder value. You can take advantage of opportunities to master new skills, work across different disciplines, move into new challenges and develop a robust understanding of different industries.

As SAP Analytics consultant, you will deliver innovative analytical/reporting solutions utilizing the most current versions of SAP solutions to ensure successful SAP implementations by collaborating with cross functional business and technical resources.

This position requires excellent verbal and written communication skills, ability to interact with both business and technical stakeholders of client companies and a proven track record designing and implementing S/4 HANA embedded analytics, SAP HANA Cloud Solutions, SAP Datasphere & SAP Analytics Cloud (SAC). You will be a team player, proactive, an effective communicator with ability to work independently.

Required Technical and Professional Expertise


5+ years’ experience in implementing SAP Analytical/Reporting for various industry sectors
Technical understanding of one or more SAP software tools for analytics such as SAP Datasphere, SAP S/4 HANA Embedded Analytcis, SAP Analytics Cloud, SAP HANA Cloud.
Experience in the remediation of SAP BWonHANA or SAP BW/4 HANA when ECC is migrated to S/4 HANA.
Develop functional/technical specification documents and design technical solution to support analytical/reporting deliverables
Participated in all the aspects of the project life cycle; including gathering requirements, Gap Analysis and blueprinting, system configuration, customization, testing, documenting, deployment and training end-users
min. 2 full cycle implementations of SAP S/4 HANA Embedded Analytics and minimum one implementation of SAP Datasphere, SAP Analytics Cloud and SAP HANA Cloud in production environment
Experience with data acquisition tools (BODS, SLT, SDI, ODQ/ODP, CDS, Cloud Connectors...)
Working knowledge of SAP implementation activities from an Activate perspective, Prepare, Explore, Realize Build, Realize Test, Deploy and Support to Sustainment.


Preferred Technical And Professional Expertise


SAP/ABAP debugging/development skills
Professional certificate related to the relevant domain (SAC, HANA)
Experience in Agile and Dev/Ops methodologies, e.g. Scrum or SAFe
Good knowledge of KPI identification approaches, evaluation of BI/EDW Maturity as well as implement a BI/EDW Governance and BI/EDW Roadmap
Develop and support Analytics Governance implementation and underlying organization model
Enhanced Reliability Security Clearance
