Role Summary

As a Data Analyst for Payroll Implementation, your primary responsibility will be to analyze and interpret data related to the implementation of a new payroll system. You will work closely with the project team to gather and validate data, perform data cleansing and transformation, and provide insights and recommendations based on your analysis.

Key Responsibilities

 Collaborate with the project team to understand data requirements for the payroll system implementation.
 Gather, validate, and analyze data from various sources, ensuring data accuracy and completeness.
 Perform data cleansing and transformation to ensure data consistency and integrity.
 Develop and maintain data models, reports, and dashboards to visualize and present data analysis findings.
 Identify trends, patterns, and anomalies in data, and provide insights and recommendations to optimize payroll processes.
 Work closely with stakeholders to understand their data analysis needs and provide customized reports and analysis.
 Collaborate with IT teams to ensure data integration and migration from legacy systems to the new payroll system.
 Perform data validation and reconciliation to ensure data accuracy and consistency between different systems.
 Assist in the development and implementation of data quality control measures to ensure data integrity.
 Stay updated with industry best practices and trends in data analysis and implement them in the payroll implementation process.



Key Qualifications/Requirements

 Bachelor's degree in Data Science, Statistics, Computer Science, or a related field.
 Proven experience as a data analyst or similar role, preferably in the payroll domain.
 Strong proficiency in data analysis and visualization tools such as SQL, Excel, Power BI, or Tableau.
 Excellent data manipulation and data cleansing skills.
 Knowledge of database management systems, data warehousing, and data integration concepts.
 Strong analytical and problem-solving skills.
 Ability to interpret complex data and present insights in a clear and concise manner.
 Strong attention to detail and accuracy in data analysis.
 Ability to work effectively in a team and collaborate with cross-functional stakeholders.
 Knowledge of payroll processes, systems, and compliance requirements is an asset.



Additional Information

Background: 

The OHA’s Policy and Advocacy division focuses on policy and advocacy, strategic communications, and research and analysis. The team strives to be proactive on core issues affecting Ontario hospitals by engaging in advocacy, shaping legislative and regulatory changes, providing advice and guidance on a diverse range of policy matters, and communicating hospitals’ concerns and challenges to government and the public. The OHA is also attuned to the broader strategic questions facing the future of the province’s health care system and we work to ensure Ontario’s hospitals have a voice in shaping this longer-term vision.

The OHA is looking for a proactive long-term thinker to provide timely innovative delivery of accurate, high value, and actionable integrated advanced hospital financial analytics and insights to drive decision making. You are a great listener and have a communication style, energy, and self-confidence to motivate people. You will be leading the financial analyses in OHA’s research, analysis and policy development related to hospital financial matters.

The Position:
 
Reporting to the Chief, Financial Policy, Research and Performance, the Financial Analytics and System Performance Consultant will conduct leading analyses on hospital and health system performance and contribute to OHA’s strategic policy development, analysis on hospital funding and financial sustainability. You will work closely with senior officials from hospitals, government, and other health service providers to influence Ontario’s Patient-Based Funding methodologies. This role will focus on converting detailed data into a compelling story to drive the OHA’s advocacy. Responsibilities include:

Analyzing issues affecting the financial health of hospitals and providing policy advice to OHA and hospital leadership.
Preparing presentations, policy papers and submissions on hospital funding and financial issues.
Liaising with Ministry of Health and Ontario Health - LHINs related to hospital funding and financial issues.
Leading and / or representing OHA on various external committees.
Conducting methodological reviews of the existing funding approaches, including performing relevant data analyses and literature reviews.
Communicating with hospitals on funding and financial matters to advise on financial issues and to collect input/feedback from hospitals.

The Candidate:

The ideal candidate possesses an Undergraduate or Post Graduate degree in a health discipline with experience in hospital funding and demonstrates post-qualifying experience in a health care setting. Hospital experience with a professional accounting designation (CMA, CGA or CA) or equivalent is an asset. Over five years of experience in a decision support or analytical environment; healthcare experience is preferred. Additional qualifications include:

Knowledge and understanding of health system funding concepts and practices including hospital reporting requirements.
Strong analytical and research skills with experience with working experience with various health care administrative datasets (e.g., Ministry - IntelliHealth, Ontario Hospital Reporting System (OHRS), Ontario Case Costing (OCC) and the Canadian Institute for Health Administration datasets – DAD, NACRS, CCRS, OMHRS, NRS, IDS, and CIHI Portal for benchmarking purposes.
Ability to analyze data and present complex financial and statistical information and to develop recommendations in an easy-to-understand manner.
Provide support in a variety of analytical needs including development of robust analytical plans, statistical analysis, key performance indicators, benchmarking, data visualizations, and routine and ad hoc reporting.
Advanced proficiency in Microsoft Excel, SQL, and Power BI.

You have excellent interpersonal, facilitation, and written and verbal communication skills; strong research, analytical and policy skills; and proven project management experience. Working in a team environment, you will be a highly motivated self-starter who enjoys working in a fast-paced environment, is able to build successful working relationships with a variety of stakeholders and enjoys turning detailed data into a story.

The ideal candidate might be described as dynamic, positive, collaborative, persuasive, resilient, driven and results oriented.

About the job
IPEX est l’un des principaux fournisseurs de systèmes intégrés de tuyauteries thermoplastiques en Amérique du Nord. Nous avons pour mission de bâtir un avenir meilleur en connectant les gens avec l’eau et l’énergie.

Nous avons présentement une opportunité en tant qu’analyste/développeur de rapports BI. Ce rôle est basé à notre siège social à l’Île-des-Sœurs, à Montréal, Québec, et relève du Directeur principal, livraison des applications des TI, MIS.

Ne manquez pas l’opportunité de joindre une grande famille de professionnels centrée sur les gens, leaders à l’esprit agile, entrepreneurs dans l’âme qui aiment défier le statu quo.

Description Du Poste

L’analyste de systèmes, ou développeur de données, dirigera la conception, l’élaboration et la proposition de solutions de rapports de données et de tableaux de bord (en fonction de l’analyse fonctionnelle et des exigences commerciales) et participera aux tâches de développement, à la mise à l’essai, au déploiement et au soutien de diverses solutions de rapports de données afin d’atteindre les objectifs de la compagnie. La personne retenue collaborera étroitement avec les analystes d’affaires et fonctionnels.

Activités principales

Stratégie et planification

Aider à la restructuration, à la conception et au développement de nouveaux rapports et tableaux de bord, ainsi qu’à l’amélioration des rapports existants.
Assurer la compatibilité et l’interopérabilité des rapports et de l’environnement du tableau de bord.
Examiner et analyser l’efficacité des rapports existants et élaborer des stratégies pour les améliorer ou mieux les exploiter.
Recommander des techniques et des stratégies d’optimisation des rapports et des tableaux de bord visant à améliorer la performance et les processus du système.
Promouvoir les concepts de développement agile et les techniques d’élaboration des pratiques d’excellence.
Faire preuve d’esprit d’équipe au sein d’un groupe de développeurs de données – collaborer, être à l’écoute, soutenir et échanger des idées efficacement en équipe.
Capacité à appliquer un raisonnement hautement intellectuel et aptitudes en résolution de problèmes. Analyser les renseignements et les situations pour susciter de nouvelles idées et perspectives et élaborer des solutions pratiques.

Acquisition et déploiement

Concevoir, développer et coder de nouveaux rapports et tableaux de bord afin d’améliorer la fonctionnalité du système.
Élaborer et mettre en œuvre des procédures de test afin d’assurer la qualité de la programmation et la fonctionnalité du système.
Gérer soi-même ses activités et livrables.
Préparer des spécifications techniques et contribuer à la création de manuels de documentation technique et fonctionnelle.

Gestion opérationnelle

Créer des modèles de systèmes, des spécifications, des diagrammes et des graphiques pour guider les développeurs de données.
Coordonner et réaliser des tests approfondis, y compris l’évaluation par les utilisateurs finaux pour les rapports modifiés et nouveaux.

Connaissances et compétences nécessaires

Baccalauréat en informatique ou dans une discipline technique connexe.
Plus de 5 ans d’expérience intermédiaire dans l’environnement des données et les applications de données; expérience professionnelle en tant qu’analyste fonctionnel ou développeur.
Connaissance solide des outils suivants :
SQL
Power BI
Technologie d’ETC : SSIS
Technologie de veille stratégique : SSRS, SSAS.
Niveau intermédiaire en .NET et expérience de programmation avec Python.
Niveau intermédiaire en intégration et en élaboration de systèmes d’interrogation dans Excel.
Niveau de base en base de données Microsoft SQL Server et de MS Azure.
Capacité à développer et à mettre en œuvre un code SQL de haute qualité dans les délais impartis.
Bilinguisme français et anglais.
Capacité à communiquer efficacement avec un public technique et non-technique, à l’oral comme à l’écrit.
Proactivité, autonomie, supervision minimale requise.
Esprit analytique, innovant et créatif. Capacité à faire valoir ses propres idées.
Soucis de précision et de qualité du travail.
Capacité à travailler harmonieusement avec les autres, particulièrement en tant que membre d’une équipe.
Capacité à respecter les délais et à mener plusieurs tâches de front.
Capacité à gérer des priorités concurrentes dans un milieu complexe.

Affirm is reinventing credit to make it more honest and friendly, giving consumers the flexibility to buy now and pay later without any hidden fees or compounding interest.

We are seeking a highly skilled and experienced Senior Analyst to join our dynamic team, focusing on causal inference and the development of MVP versions of machine learning (ML) models. This role is pivotal in leveraging data science to understand the why behind our data, enabling informed decision-making and driving innovative solutions. The ideal candidate will have a strong background in statistical analysis, causal inference methodologies, and experience in building and iterating on ML models in a fast-paced environment.

What You Will Do

Causal Inference Analysis: Apply advanced causal inference techniques to uncover the underlying mechanisms and effects within our datasets, facilitating a deeper understanding of our data's drivers.
ML Modeling: Develop and refine MVP versions of ML models, focusing on rapid prototyping to test hypotheses and assess potential impact, with an eye towards scalability and integration into larger systems.
Cross-Functional Collaboration: Work closely with product, engineering, and business teams to define problem statements, identify data needs, and implement solutions that align with organizational goals.
Data Strategy Development: Contribute to the creation and execution of a comprehensive data strategy, emphasizing causal analysis and ML applications to support data-driven decision-making.
Insights Communication: Clearly communicate complex analytical findings and model outcomes to non-technical stakeholders, translating data insights into actionable business recommendations.

What We Look For

3+ years of experience in data analysis, with a strong focus on causal inference and ML modeling.
Proficiency in statistical software (R, Python) and familiarity with ML libraries (e.g., scikit-learn, TensorFlow).
Solid understanding of statistical modeling, experimental design, and A/B testing frameworks.
Exceptional analytical, problem-solving, and communication skills.
Bachelor's or Master's degree in Statistics, Computer Science, Economics, or a related quantitative field.

This role is also interpreting, summarizing, creating, and maintaining statistical data files; writing reports and dashboards on trends and analysis; contributing to the development and monitoring of performance indicators and systems.

 Apply appropriate statistical techniques to interpret data and develop statistical methodology. 
 Compile and analyze data to interpret trends, fluctuations, and other changes. 
 Research problems to determine the required data for specific questions. 
 Support team members in interpreting collected data and categorizing findings. 
 Prepare detailed reports for management and other departments. 
 Define and utilize statistical methods to solve industry-specific problems. 
 Monitor database information, conduct data audits, and corrections to ensure data integrity. 
 Provide strategic guidance based on statistical analysis to improve decision-making. 
 Apply advanced statistical methods such as regression analysis, clustering, factor analysis, time series analysis, and machine learning algorithms. 
 Conduct exploratory data analysis to uncover patterns and outliers and identify potential data quality issues. 
 Develop predictive and prescriptive models to uncover patterns, correlations, and trends within complex datasets. 
 Apply sampling techniques to determine significant subsets for analysis. 
 Manage information in accordance with industry regulations and organization standards. 
 Ensure the quality and confidentiality of data.

We are seeking a highly skilled and experienced Senior Analyst to join our dynamic team, focusing on causal inference and the development of MVP versions of machine learning (ML) models. This role is pivotal in leveraging data science to understand the why behind our data, enabling informed decision-making and driving innovative solutions. The ideal candidate will have a strong background in statistical analysis, causal inference methodologies, and experience in building and iterating on ML models in a fast-paced environment.

What You Will Do

Causal Inference Analysis: Apply advanced causal inference techniques to uncover the underlying mechanisms and effects within our datasets, facilitating a deeper understanding of our data's drivers.
ML Modeling: Develop and refine MVP versions of ML models, focusing on rapid prototyping to test hypotheses and assess potential impact, with an eye towards scalability and integration into larger systems.
Cross-Functional Collaboration: Work closely with product, engineering, and business teams to define problem statements, identify data needs, and implement solutions that align with organizational goals.
Data Strategy Development: Contribute to the creation and execution of a comprehensive data strategy, emphasizing causal analysis and ML applications to support data-driven decision-making.
Insights Communication: Clearly communicate complex analytical findings and model outcomes to non-technical stakeholders, translating data insights into actionable business recommendations.

What We Look For

3+ years of experience in data analysis, with a strong focus on causal inference and ML modeling.
Proficiency in statistical software (R, Python) and familiarity with ML libraries (e.g., scikit-learn, TensorFlow).
Solid understanding of statistical modeling, experimental design, and A/B testing frameworks.
Exceptional analytical, problem-solving, and communication skills.

Our Values
At TD we're guided by our purpose is to enrich the lives of our customers, communities and colleagues, and share a set of values that shape our culture and guide our behavior. In exchange for how our colleagues show up to help TD succeed, we are committed to delivering a colleague experience grounded in Impact, Growth and a Culture of Care. No matter where you work across TD, we empower you to make an impact at work and in your community, explore and grow your career and be part of our caring and inclusive culture.

Making Your Well-being a Priority
A supportive culture that promotes colleague well-being is core to who we are. At TD, we focus on total well-being with extensive programs to help colleagues assess, manage, and improve their well-being across four core pillars — physical, financial, social and mental/emotional. In addition, we champion a safe and inclusive work environment so colleagues feel a sense of belonging and feel supported in their personal and professional growth. Through our focus on well-being, we know that we can help our colleagues thrive, contribute to our culture of care, and support better business outcomes, because when colleagues feel their best, they're more likely to do their best.

Our Total Rewards Package
Our Total Rewards package reflects the investment we make in our colleagues to help them, and their families achieve their well-being goals. Total Rewards at TD includes a base salary, variable compensation, and several other key plans such as health and well-being benefits including medical, dental, vision & mental health coverage, savings and retirement programs, paid time off, banking benefits and discounts, career development, and reward and recognition programs.

How We Work
At TD, we believe in-person connections fuel collaboration and collective creativity. Our workplace experience empowers colleagues to do great work side-by-side at TD locations, while offering flexibility to work remotely where it makes sense for the work and team. Our teams work in one of three workplace models: Hybrid, Onsite and Primarily Remote. Wherever our colleagues are working, they’ll always have access to the TD community and experience our culture of care.

Who We Are
TD is one of the world's leading global financial institutions and is the fifth largest bank in North America by branches. Every day, we deliver legendary customer experiences to over 27 million households and businesses in Canada, the United States and around the world. More than 95,000 TD colleagues bring their skills, talent, and creativity to the Bank, those we serve, and the economies we support. We are guided by our vision to Be the Better Bank and our purpose to enrich the lives of our customers, communities and colleagues.

Job Description

About this Role

This role is responsible for monitoring fraud trends, investigating emerging threats and quickly developing and deploying new strategies to manage those threats. 
The strategist 
Must balance loss decisions with the impact to operational teams and the customer experience. 
Is expected to develop and apply deep fraud and process expertise, and to leverage sophisticated tools/detection systems to manage risk/reward balance. 

The successful candidate will work collaboratively with a diverse team of operational agents, Fraud solution developers, data scientists, business insights analysts and subject matter experts and applies fraud business expertise leveraging advanced tools and detection systems to manage risk appropriately. The incumbent will be accountable for loss and customer experience targets.


Accountabilities:

Fraud Loss Management
Reviews daily fraud attacks to create segmentation and develop/implement fraud strategies while balancing the impact to the operational teams and customer experience
Design and develop advanced analytics tools to derive business insights from data and information
Makes adjustments to shifting network rules, liability requirements or other exogenous factors
Executes strategy design and configuration in all fraud prevention platforms (e.g. Faclon, TSYS, FIS, SQN, PRM, Citadel, DPS, VCas, Avant, Experian, Transunion), in alignment with the Change Management protocols
Supports case valuation and prioritization to optimize fraud management
Become a subject matter expert on the end-to-end operational process, transaction liability and regulatory requirements

Process Support
Produce timely diagnostics to identify system, strategy and operational issues
Participates in defect analysis to identify and remediate fraud coverage gaps
Identify and assess new developing fraud trends as they evolve
Participates in the creation of monitoring and reporting by defining requirements and performing validation

Partner Support
Maintain strong relationships with internal stakeholders such as Fraud Operations
Support the continuous improvement agenda for our operational partners

Demonstrated analytical, modeling and problem solving skills 
Creative, Critical, Conceptual thinker, ability to wade through data and arrive at conclusions
Ability to communicate strategy analysis to both technical and non-technical team members, either verbally or via documentation

More About Hopper

At Hopper, we are on a mission to become the leading travel platform globally – powering Hopper’s mobile app, website and our B2B business, HTS (Hopper Technology Solutions). By leveraging massive amounts of data and advanced machine learning algorithms, Hopper combines its world-class travel agency offering with proprietary fintech products to bring transparency, flexibility and savings to travelers globally. We have developed several unique fintech solutions that address everything from pricing volatility to trip disruptions – helping people travel better and save more on their trips.

The Hopper platform serves hundreds of millions of travelers globally and continues to capture market share around the world. Ranked the third largest online travel agency in North America, the Hopper app has been downloaded over 120 million times and has become largely popular among younger travelers – with 70% of its users being Gen Z and millennials.

While everyone knows us as the Gen Z and Millennial travel app, Hopper has evolved to become much more than that. In recent years, we’ve grown into a global travel agency and travel fintech provider that powers some of the world’s largest brands.

Through HTS, our B2B division, the company supercharges its partners’ direct channels by integrating our fintech products on their sites or powering end-to-end travel portals. Today, our partners include leading travel brands like Capital One, Nubank, Air Canada and many more.

Here are just a few stats that demonstrate the company’s recent growth:

Comment start Hopper sells billion Comment end s worth of travel and travel fintech every year. In 2023, over 1.3 billion trips were planned through the Hopper app and our HTS partnerships.

Our fintech products – including Price Freeze, Flexibility for Any Reason and Flight Disruption Assistance – have exceptionally strong CSAT because the terms are always clear, and customers receive instant, no-questions-asked resolutions.

Almost 30% of our app customers purchase at least one fintech product when making a booking; and consumers are 1.6x more likely to repurchase if they add fintech to their booking vs if they booked just travel.

Given the success of its fintech products, Hopper launched a B2B initiative, HTS (Hopper Technology Solutions), which represents more than 50% of the business.

Through HTS, any travel provider (airlines, hotels, banks, travel agencies, etc.) can integrate and seamlessly distribute Hopper’s fintech or travel inventory on their direct channels. As its first HTS partnership, the company partnered with Capital One to co-develop Capital One Travel, a new travel portal designed specifically for cardholders. Other HTS partners include Air Canada, Uber, CommBank, Nubank, Flair Airlines with many more in the pipeline.

Featured in Apple’s Best of the App Store list of Essential Travel Apps in 2023 and recognized by the likes of Fast Company’s Most Innovative Companies, Hopper has been downloaded over 120 million times and continues to have millions of new installs each month. Hopper is now the #3 largest online travel agency in North America and 70% of our app customers are Gen-Z and millennials travelers.

Hopper has raised over $750 million USD of private capital and is backed by some of the largest institutional investors and banks in the world. Hopper is primed to continue its acceleration as the world’s fastest-growing mobile-first travel marketplace.

Who You'll Work With

Are you passionate about the future of Big Data in Finance?

If yes, we are the team for you. We, the Risk & Performance Analytics team within the Finance division is a key partner to the investment and risk team’s at OTPP. We are a team of professionals with multifaceted backgrounds (CFA, FRM, MBA, MMF) providing middle office services including performance measurement and risk attribution. We work with over a billion numbers a day and publish investment and risk metrics across asset mix, performance return, market risk, counterparty credit risk, liquidity and leverage risk to facilitate the fund’s investment decisions.

You will report to the Senior Manager, Risk & Performance Analytics and work with a team of passionate professionals to constantly challenge status quo and improve the portfolio and risk reporting and attribution practices at OTPP. You will be exposed to a broad range of asset classes, from public to private, and products, from vanilla to exotic, to learn how a sophisticated world class pension is run. While doing this you will apply your knowledge in math/computer science/business in a hands-on environment to develop skills in Bloomberg, SQL, VBA ,Python and PowerBI.

You will develop, and maintain relationships with stakeholders across the Investment, Risk, Finance and Enterprise Operation divisions while working in a collaborative culture.

What You'll Do

We are looking for 1 new graduates to join our risk reporting team and total fund reporting team under Risk & Performance Analytics. Typical responsibilities include, but are not limited to:

Ensure that data for the total fund and risk system is collected, input, and validated in an efficient manner and any issues arising from the processes are either resolved or escalated as required
Calculate and generate portfolio exposure reporting at total fund level, including but not limited to the fund’s asset mix, currency mix, country exposure, liquidity and leverage risk etc at portfolio and total fund level
Produce counterparty risk reports across business line and at total fund level and conduct factor and trade attribution analysis on material day over day exposure and VaR movements
Collaborate with internal and external collateral management team to oversee and resolve margin disputes caused by risk modelling issues
Perform credit monitoring of OTPP’s counterparties
Monitor investment exposure and risk usage against board investment policy limit and escalate as required
Maintain and enhance the business intelligence reporting suite and various analysis tools developed in-house to facilitate deeper understanding of portfolio and risk movement
Supporting the development and testing of risk model enhancements and reporting improvements

What You'll Need

University degree in a quantitative discipline such as Math, Statistics, Actuarial Science, Finance, Economics, or a related field
Prior coop or intern experience in risk management and/or investment reporting function is a strong plus
Hands-on working experience in one or more of these applications - Excel, SQL, VBA, Python, Power BI, with a desire to streamline and automate existing processes
Knowledge of capital market products, such as bonds and derivatives
An aptitude to learn with strong intellectual curiosity

More About Hopper

At Hopper, we are on a mission to become the leading travel platform globally – powering Hopper’s mobile app, website and our B2B business, HTS (Hopper Technology Solutions). By leveraging massive amounts of data and advanced machine learning algorithms, Hopper combines its world-class travel agency offering with proprietary fintech products to bring transparency, flexibility and savings to travelers globally. We have developed several unique fintech solutions that address everything from pricing volatility to trip disruptions – helping people travel better and save more on their trips.

The Hopper platform serves hundreds of millions of travelers globally and continues to capture market share around the world. Ranked the third largest online travel agency in North America, the Hopper app has been downloaded over 120 million times and has become largely popular among younger travelers – with 70% of its users being Gen Z and millennials.

While everyone knows us as the Gen Z and Millennial travel app, Hopper has evolved to become much more than that. In recent years, we’ve grown into a global travel agency and travel fintech provider that powers some of the world’s largest brands.

Our fintech products – including Price Freeze, Flexibility for Any Reason and Flight Disruption Assistance – have exceptionally strong CSAT because the terms are always clear, and customers receive instant, no-questions-asked resolutions.

Through HTS, any travel provider (airlines, hotels, banks, travel agencies, etc.) can integrate and seamlessly distribute Hopper’s fintech or travel inventory on their direct channels. Profil clé 
Vous êtes un analyste d’affaire ayant d’excellentes compétences techniques et êtes passionné de l’intelligence artificielle? Vous aspirez à contribuer à des projets ambitieux et novateur? 
Vous êtes au bon endroit! 

SIGMA-RH détient une équipe d’experts collaborant vers un objectif commun, soit celui de prôner l’excellence à travers l’offre d’une solution SIRH complète et dans l’intégralité de ses opérations. L’utilisation de technologies émergentes fait intégralement partie du quotidien de nos experts, afin d’accompagner nos clients tout au long des décisions stratégiques reliées aux ressources humaines. 

Vos responsabilités 
En tant qu'analyste d'affaires TI, vous aurez l'opportunité de participer activement à la modernisation de notre solution en mettant en place différent outils d’intelligence artificielle. 

Voici les défis qui vous attendent 
Définir, documenter, modéliser et valider les besoins d’affaires
Traduire les besoins d’affaires en requis fonctionnel et techniques à l’aide des techniques appropriées (ex. Processes mapping, Data flow diagram, ERD, User Story, Use Case Modelling, etc.)
Participer à la création, au découpage, à la priorisation et à la documentation du carnet de produit avec l’équipe de réalisation
Analyser et interpréter des ensembles de données complexes pour aider à la prise de décision
Documenter les apis d’IA externes qui peuvent être utilisées et effectuer la recherche de modèles
Collaborer avec les équipes d’ingénierie pour intégrer et déployer des modèles d’intelligences artificielle
Effectuer des analyses statistiques et fournir des rapports sur les résultats
Maintenir à jour les connaissances sur les dernières tendances et technologies en matière d’intelligence artificielle et documenter pour usage interne

Vos compétences et qualifications 
Détenir une formation universitaire et/ou une expérience d’au moins 5 ans dans un rôle pertinent (Analyste d’affaires TI / Analyste fonctionnel, Product Owner, etc.)
Avoir un minimum de 3 ans d’expériences en APIs d’IA ( Openai, Azure etc.)
Expérience concrète dans un contexte de développement logiciel axé sur l’intelligence artificielle
Expérience des techniques de traitement du langage naturel (NLP), telles que la classification de textes. 
Solide compréhension des concepts et algorithmes de l'IA, y compris l'apprentissage supervisé et non supervisé, les réseaux de neurones et l'apprentissage par renforcement
Solides compétences en résolution de problèmes et en pensée analytique
Maîtrise des concepts et des approches agiles.
Bilinguisme fonctionnel

About the job
Lieu: Laval, Quebec


Type de poste: Poste permanent à temps plein


À propos de Glencore:


Glencore est l’une des plus grandes sociétés du monde dans les ressources naturelles diversifiées. Elle est aussi une importante entreprise de production et de commercialisation de plus de 60 produits de base. Nos opérations regroupent environ 150 sites miniers et métallurgiques, installations pétrolières agricoles - étayées par un réseau mondial. Notre mission consiste à offrir, en nous acquittant de nos responsabilités sociales, les produits de base qui font évoluer le quotidien. Nous avons 135 000 employés, qui sont au cœur de notre entreprise, et nous offrons à nos employés la possibilité de développer et croître leur savoir-faire et de progresser dans leurs carrières.
La division cuivre – Amérique du Nord et Philippines de Glencore est l’un des principaux producteurs de cuivre affiné et de métaux critiques mondiaux. Nos opérations comprennent 6 sites industriels, incluant des fonderies, affineries et sites de recyclage.



Rejoignez-nous et grandissons ensemble.


À propos du poste:

Relevant du responsable des services transactionnels régionaux pour le processus d’approvisionnement au paiement (P2P), vous serez responsable de la gouvernance, des indicateurs de rendement clés, de la production de rapports et des processus opérationnels.
Le spécialiste en gouvernance et rapports joue un rôle de facilitateur et de catalyseur en veillant à ce que les processus de gouvernance favorisent la transparence, la responsabilité et une prise de décision efficace au sein du groupe des services transactionnels pour le processus d’approvisionnement au paiement (P2P).
Élaborer et tenir à jour des indicateurs de rendement clés et des rapports connexes concernant les processus d’approvisionnement au paiement (P2P) et les données sur le rendement, les mesures et les tendances connexes au sein de la fonction des services transactionnels, à des fins d’information et de prise de décision pour la direction et les parties prenantes.


Plus spécifiquement, vous aurez à:


Organiser des réunions en élaborant des ordres du jour, en préparant et en rassemblant les documents nécessaires, et en assurant la liaison avec les parties prenantes en vue de leur implication.
Diriger les discussions des réunions de gouvernance en respectant les ordres du jour, en guidant la prise de décision et en favorisant le consensus, afin d’obtenir des résultats productifs pour l’équipe.
Rédiger les procès-verbaux, les décisions et les plans d’action pour référence ultérieure, en veillant à ce que les résultats des réunions, les décisions et les mesures à prendre soient communiqués en temps utile aux parties prenantes concernées.
Offrir des conseils, des ateliers ou des séances de formation sur les principes et les pratiques de gouvernance aux membres de l’équipe.
Évaluer l’efficience et l’efficacité de la structure de gouvernance et recommander des améliorations.
Identifier les possibilités d’amélioration des processus dans le cadre de la gouvernance.
Produire des rapports sur les indicateurs de rendement clés afin de garantir l’exactitude de l’extraction et de la fonctionnalité des données, en vue de soutenir les cycles de rapports financiers.
Recueillir des données quantitatives à partir de plateformes telles que SAP afin de créer des rapports cohérents et précis sur les processus d’approvisionnement au paiement (P2P).
Élaborer et tenir à jour des rapports sur les indicateurs de rendement clés qui reflètent l’aspect financier et de performance des processus d’approvisionnement au paiement (P2P) en respectant les exigences en matière de conformité et de processus internes.


Compétences:


Baccalauréat ou maîtrise dans un domaine pertinent tel que comptabilité, finances, gestion des opérations ou gestion de la chaîne d’approvisionnement.
Plus de cinq ans d’expérience dans un rôle similaire avec une maîtrise des plateformes SAP et Power BI. Expérience avec la plateforme Coupa Procure-to-Pay, un atout.
Volonté de se tenir au courant des meilleures pratiques et des technologies émergentes.
Capacité à analyser des données, à identifier des tendances et à extraire des informations significatives pour éclairer la prise de décision en mettant l’accent sur l’obtention de résultats.
Maîtrise de l’élaboration et de la mise à jour de rapports, de tableaux de bord et d’indicateurs de rendement clés (IRC) en vue d’une communication efficace des mesures de performance.
Compréhension des principes de gouvernance et des normes de conformité.



Langues : Français et anglais (maîtrise obligatoire)


Voyage : Des déplacements régionaux et dans le monde entier peuvent être nécessaires.


Ce que nous offrons:



Culture professionnelle favorisant la sécurité, l’intégrité, la responsabilité, l’ouverture d’esprit, la simplicité et l’entrepreneuriat
Régime d’avantages sociaux concurrentiel et complet
Horaires de travail souples
Programmes de mieux être des employés
Perspectives de développement professionnel

Location: Laval, Quebec
Job type: Permanent full-time position

About Glencore:

Glencore is one of the world’s largest diversified natural resources companies. It is also a major producer and marketer of more than 60 commodities. Our operations include approximately 150 mining and metallurgical sites and agricultural oil facilities supported by a global network. Our mission is to provide the commodities that make everyday life better, in a socially responsible way. Our people are fundamental to our success. We employ some 135,000 people and offer them the opportunity to develop and grow their skills and careers.

About the role:

Reporting to the Regions Procure-To-Pay (P2P) Transactional Services Leader, you will be responsible for governance, KPIs, reporting and business processes.
The Governance and Reporting specialist acts as a facilitator and enabler, ensuring that the governance processes promote transparency, accountability, and effective decision-making within the P2P transactional services group.
Develop and maintain KPI and related reports relating to P2P processes and related performance data, metrics, and trends within the transactional services function for management and stakeholder information and decision-making purposes.

More specifically, you will:

 Orchestrate meetings by developing agendas, preparing, and assembling necessary documents, and liaising with stakeholders for their engagement.
 Lead governance meeting discussions aligned with agendas, guiding decision-making, and fostering consensus, driving productive outcomes for the team.
Record meeting minutes, decisions, and action plans for future reference, ensuring timely sharing of meeting outcomes, decisions, and action items with relevant stakeholders.
Offer guidance, workshops, or training sessions on governance principles and practices for team members.
Assess the efficiency and efficacy of governance structure and recommend improvements.
Identify areas for process enhancement within the governance framework.
Operate within KPI reporting frameworks to ensure accurate data extraction and functionality, supporting financial reporting cycles.
Gather quantitative data from enterprise systems like SAP to create consistent and accurate reports for P2P (Procure-to-Pay) processes.
Develop and maintain KPI reports reflecting P2P financials and related performance, meeting compliance and internal process requirements.
Review and amend reports as needed to meet evolving circumstances and stakeholder requirements.



Skills:

A bachelor’s or master’s degree in a relevant field such as accounting, finance, operations management, or supply chain management.
5+ years in a similar role with proficiency in SAP, Power BI. Experience in Coupa Procure-to-Pay Platform environment is an advantage.
Willingness to stay updated on best practices and emerging technologies.
Ability to analyze data, identify trends, and extract meaningful insights to inform decision-making with a focus on achieving results.
Proficiency in developing and maintaining reports, dashboards, and key performance indicators (KPIs) for effective communication of performance metrics.
Understanding of governance principles and compliance standards.
Adept at identifying issues, proposing solutions, and implementing improvements to enhance governance and reporting processes.





Languages: French and English (Fluency is Mandatory)

Travel: Within the region and globally may be required.

What we offer:
A work culture that promotes safety, integrity, responsibility, open-mindedness, simplicity, and entrepreneurship.
A competitive, comprehensive benefits plan.
Flexible working hours.
Employee wellness programs.
Professional development opportunities.

About the job:
GREAT CAREER OPPORTUNITY
SENIOR BUSINESS /HRIS ANALYST/SENIOR BUSINESS ANALYST
Our client ,a highly respected Canadian Organization, is one of North America’s leading apparel retailers in North America has granted us the mandate to search and recruit a Senior HRIS Business Analyst .
This Organization is committed to creating a culture where people feel valued and inspired to achieve results. We attract and nurture the best people by providing leadership opportunities, career development and continuous learning. They are committed to leading by example and with integrity. They treat people with respect and dignity and promote the benefits of diversity. That is the Philosophy of our client.
 A.  Role Summary:
As member of The Financial Department team, the successful Senior HRIS Business Analyst candidate needs to be experienced with HRIS and payroll systems, ideally with Ceridian Dayforce.
You will be responsible :
· To be a system advisor
· To handle system implementation and integration (updates or new configuration required by SME)
· To provide reporting and analytics (The Organization has just implemented, need help with current documentation, which Ceitidan lacked in providing)
· To ensure compliance of the system (standardization, gatekeeper)
· To ensure training and education (new features or new users)
· This senior position required from the selected candidate to be extremely organized and very proactive
 B. Role Description
This is a full-time on-site role for a Senior HRIS Business Analyst / Senior Business Intelligence Analyst located in Toronto, ON. As a Senior HRIS Business Analyst / Senior Business Intelligence Analyst, you will be responsible for analyzing, designing, and implementing HR information systems that support HR business processes. You will also collaborate with cross-functional teams to gather requirements, design and develop reports, provide analytical insights, and enhance data visualization. Additionally, you will participate in data quality audits, data integration, and data quality improvement projects, and provide technical support for HR system inquiries.
 C. Qualifications
Bachelor's degree or higher in Human Resources, Business Administration, Computer Science, Information Systems Management, or a related field.
Minimum of 5 years of experience as an HRIS Business Analyst or BI Analyst
Strong technical skills in SQL, data modeling, and data visualization.
Experience with HRIS systems such as Workday, PeopleSoft, or Oracle E-Business suite
Experience analyzing and designing solutions for complex integration and data quality improvement projects.
Competent in data modeling concepts and technologies
Experience with Agile/Scrum development methodologies.
Ability to work both independently and in a team environment, with strong problem-solving and analytical skills.
Excellent verbal and written communication and interpersonal skills.

About the job
Affirm is reinventing credit to make it more honest and friendly, giving consumers the flexibility to buy now and pay later without any hidden fees or compounding interest.

We are seeking a highly skilled and experienced Senior Analyst to join our dynamic team, focusing on causal inference and the development of MVP versions of machine learning (ML) models. This role is pivotal in leveraging data science to understand the why behind our data, enabling informed decision-making and driving innovative solutions. The ideal candidate will have a strong background in statistical analysis, causal inference methodologies, and experience in building and iterating on ML models in a fast-paced environment.

What You Will Do

Causal Inference Analysis: Apply advanced causal inference techniques to uncover the underlying mechanisms and effects within our datasets, facilitating a deeper understanding of our data's drivers.
ML Modeling: Develop and refine MVP versions of ML models, focusing on rapid prototyping to test hypotheses and assess potential impact, with an eye towards scalability and integration into larger systems.
Cross-Functional Collaboration: Work closely with product, engineering, and business teams to define problem statements, identify data needs, and implement solutions that align with organizational goals.
Data Strategy Development: Contribute to the creation and execution of a comprehensive data strategy, emphasizing causal analysis and ML applications to support data-driven decision-making.
Insights Communication: Clearly communicate complex analytical findings and model outcomes to non-technical stakeholders, translating data insights into actionable business recommendations.

What We Look For

3+ years of experience in data analysis, with a strong focus on causal inference and ML modeling.
Proficiency in statistical software (R, Python) and familiarity with ML libraries (e.g., scikit-learn, TensorFlow).
Solid understanding of statistical modeling, experimental design, and A/B testing frameworks.
Exceptional analytical, problem-solving, and communication skills.
Bachelor's or Master's degree in Statistics, Computer Science, Economics, or a related quantitative field.

Pay Grade - CAN29

About the job
Vous jouerez un rôle essentiel dans la résolution des problèmes de données et d'ingénierie visant à améliorer les offres d'hébergement de Hopper, faisant de Hopper le meilleur endroit pour réserver des hôtels et des locations de vacances.

Ce rôle a un impact énorme sur la vision et le succès de l'entreprise. C'est une occasion unique de rejoindre l'une des équipes stratégiques d'hébergement de Hopper et d'avoir accès à des ensembles de données fascinantes et massives sur le marché et les comportements.

Votre principale responsabilité consistera à prendre en charge l'entreposage de nos données, à garantir l'accessibilité des données et à fournir des informations qui façonneront notre orientation stratégique.

Il s'agit d'une formidable occasion de croissance personnelle et comprend un potentiel élevé d'avantages sur les options d'achat d'actions avant l'introduction en bourse.

Ta routine ressemblerait à quoi?

Dans ce rôle, vous ferez partie d'une équipe transversale de chefs de produits, de scientifiques de données et d'ingénieurs qui travaillent en étroite collaboration pour faciliter les voyages et atteindre des millions d'utilisateurs dans le processus. Les responsabilités comprennent : 
Initier, développer et maintenir des pipelines de données : piloter de manière indépendante la création et la maintenance de pipelines de données essentiels à la prise de décision basée sur les données. Vous assurer que ces pipelines sont robustes, efficaces et constamment mis à jour pour fournir des informations en temps réel.
Propriété de l'entrepôt de données : Assumer pleinement la responsabilité de notre entrepôt de données, en en faisant une ressource accessible et conviviale pour les équipes de produits et les équipes commerciales. Rationaliser le stockage, la récupération et l'organisation des données pour permettre aux équipes d'obtenir des informations exploitables.
Indicateurs de performance clés et cadres d'établissement de rapports : identifier, affiner et suivre les indicateurs de performance clés (KPI) essentiels à l'évaluation de la performance de l'entreprise. Élaborer et maintenir des cadres de rapports qui permettent un suivi et des rapports continus de ces mesures.
Rapports de base pour la prise de décision : créer et gérer des systèmes de rapports de base qui pilotent à la fois les décisions opérationnelles quotidiennes et les décisions stratégiques à long terme. Veiller à ce que ces rapports fournissent des informations exploitables et soient facilement accessibles aux parties prenantes concernées.
Possibilités de croissance des revenus : en devenant un expert de nos données et en comprenant parfaitement nos clients, identifier de manière proactive de nouvelles possibilités de croissance des revenus. Collaborer avec des équipes transversales pour mettre en œuvre des stratégies qui capitalisent sur ces possibilités.
Autonomie dans la résolution de problèmes : identifier les défis liés aux données et développer des solutions créatives de manière indépendante. Démontrer une approche proactive en matière de résolution de problèmes et un engagement envers la qualité et l'exactitude des données. 
Nous recherchons une personne qui a un réel désir de passer à l'action, qui s'approprie le projet, qui s'épanouit dans l'autonomie et qui obtient des résultats.

Atouts d'une candidate idéale ou d'un candidat idéal :

Avoir un minimum de 5 années d'expérience dans un environnement à cadence rapide et où les données sont au centre du processus décisionnel
Est parfaitement bilingue anglais/français (nous travaillons à travers +22 pays!)
Possède une expérience reconnue en résolution de problèmes complexes avec une compréhension approfondie des données, des produits et de l'impact commercial
Grande attention aux détails et capacité à créer des solutions de données évolutives
Maîtrise de l'utilisation de SQL pour la création, la maintenance et l'analyse des données
A de l'expérience avec des outils de visualisation de données (Looker, Tableau, Amplitude, Big Query)
Expertise démontrée dans le maintien de la qualité, de l'intégrité et de la conformité des données aux meilleures pratiques de gouvernance des données.
A travaillé sur un produit de consommation et a expédié des modèles à fort impact à grande échelle
Forte expérience, connaissance et/ou vif intérêt pour les prix et les stocks du marché.
De solides compétences en résolution de problèmes et en pensée critique
Expérience dans le lancement, l'analyse et la mise en place de cadres pour les tests A/B.

Les Avantages De Travailler Avec Nous

Des congés payés illimités

De petites équipes dynamiques = un impact énorme

La participation à un régime d'épargne-retraite

More About Hopper

At Hopper, we are on a mission to become the leading travel platform globally – powering Hopper’s mobile app, website and our B2B business, HTS (Hopper Technology Solutions). By leveraging massive amounts of data and advanced machine learning algorithms, Hopper combines its world-class travel agency offering with proprietary fintech products to bring transparency, flexibility and savings to travelers globally. We have developed several unique fintech solutions that address everything from pricing volatility to trip disruptions – helping people travel better and save more on their trips.

The Hopper platform serves hundreds of millions of travelers globally and continues to capture market share around the world. Ranked the third largest online travel agency in North America, the Hopper app has been downloaded over 120 million times and has become largely popular among younger travelers – with 70% of its users being Gen Z and millennials.

While everyone knows us as the Gen Z and Millennial travel app, Hopper has evolved to become much more than that. In recent years, we’ve grown into a global travel agency and travel fintech provider that powers some of the world’s largest brands.

Through HTS, our B2B division, the company supercharges its partners’ direct channels by integrating our fintech products on their sites or powering end-to-end travel portals. Today, our partners include leading travel brands like Capital One, Nubank, Air Canada and many more.

Here are just a few stats that demonstrate the company’s recent growth:

Comment start Hopper sells billion Comment end s worth of travel and travel fintech every year. In 2023, over 1.3 billion trips were planned through the Hopper app and our HTS partnerships.

Our fintech products – including Price Freeze, Flexibility for Any Reason and Flight Disruption Assistance – have exceptionally strong CSAT because the terms are always clear, and customers receive instant, no-questions-asked resolutions.

Almost 30% of our app customers purchase at least one fintech product when making a booking; and consumers are 1.6x more likely to repurchase if they add fintech to their booking vs if they booked just travel.

Given the success of its fintech products, Hopper launched a B2B initiative, HTS (Hopper Technology Solutions), which represents more than 50% of the business.

Through HTS, any travel provider (airlines, hotels, banks, travel agencies, etc.) can integrate and seamlessly distribute Hopper’s fintech or travel inventory on their direct channels. As its first HTS partnership, the company partnered with Capital One to co-develop Capital One Travel, a new travel portal designed specifically for cardholders. Other HTS partners include Air Canada, Uber, CommBank, Nubank, Flair Airlines with many more in the pipeline.

Featured in Apple’s Best of the App Store list of Essential Travel Apps in 2023 and recognized by the likes of Fast Company’s Most Innovative Companies, Hopper has been downloaded over 120 million times and continues to have millions of new installs each month. Hopper is now the #3 largest online travel agency in North America and 70% of our app customers are Gen-Z and millennials travelers.

Hopper has raised over $750 million USD of private capital and is backed by some of the largest institutional investors and banks in the world. Hopper is primed to continue its acceleration as the world’s fastest-growing mobile-first travel marketplace.

Come take off with us!
About the job
Affirm is reinventing credit to make it more honest and friendly, giving consumers the flexibility to buy now and pay later without any hidden fees or compounding interest.

We are seeking a highly skilled and experienced Senior Analyst to join our dynamic team, focusing on causal inference and the development of MVP versions of machine learning (ML) models. This role is pivotal in leveraging data science to understand the why behind our data, enabling informed decision-making and driving innovative solutions. The ideal candidate will have a strong background in statistical analysis, causal inference methodologies, and experience in building and iterating on ML models in a fast-paced environment.

What You Will Do

Causal Inference Analysis: Apply advanced causal inference techniques to uncover the underlying mechanisms and effects within our datasets, facilitating a deeper understanding of our data's drivers.
ML Modeling: Develop and refine MVP versions of ML models, focusing on rapid prototyping to test hypotheses and assess potential impact, with an eye towards scalability and integration into larger systems.
Cross-Functional Collaboration: Work closely with product, engineering, and business teams to define problem statements, identify data needs, and implement solutions that align with organizational goals.
Data Strategy Development: Contribute to the creation and execution of a comprehensive data strategy, emphasizing causal analysis and ML applications to support data-driven decision-making.
Insights Communication: Clearly communicate complex analytical findings and model outcomes to non-technical stakeholders, translating data insights into actionable business recommendations.

What We Look For

3+ years of experience in data analysis, with a strong focus on causal inference and ML modeling.
Proficiency in statistical software (R, Python) and familiarity with ML libraries (e.g., scikit-learn, TensorFlow).
Solid understanding of statistical modeling, experimental design, and A/B testing frameworks.
Exceptional analytical, problem-solving, and communication skills.
Bachelor's or Master's degree in Statistics, Computer Science, Economics, or a related quantitative field.

About the job
Job Description, Revenue Operations Reporting & Analytics Analyst

Equinix is the world’s digital infrastructure company, operating 240+ data centers across the globe and providing interconnections to all the key clouds and networks. Businesses need one place to simplify and bring together fragmented, complex infrastructure that spans private and public cloud environments. Our global platform allows customers to place infrastructure wherever they need it and connect it to everything they need to succeed.

We are a fast-growing global company with 20 years of continuous growth. Through our innovative portfolio of high-performance products and services, we have created the largest, most active global ecosystem of 10,000+ companies, including 2,100 networks and 3,000+ cloud and IT service providers in 32 countries spanning six continents.

A career at Equinix means you will collaborate on work that impacts the world and be surrounded by endless opportunities to learn new skills and grow in varied directions. We embrace diversity in thought and contribution and are committed to providing an equitable work environment. that is foundational to our core values as a company and is vital to our success.

Job Summary

As a Revenue Operations Reporting & Analytics Analyst, you will work on various asks around performance management and forecasting, enabling stakeholders across the Customer Revenue Office at different levels to make informed decisions to drive revenue growth, profitability, and efficiency.

This role empowers swift responses to various data-related reporting, BI, and analytics tasks, providing timely recommendations. This includes addressing ad-hoc requests, resolving data discrepancies, generating executive reports to support decision-making, and ensuring accuracy through reconciliation and validation processes.

Day-to-day duties will require using data visualization tools to provide ad-hoc analysis, working with many stakeholders to drive a deeper understanding of performance and productivity, and surfacing insights.

Responsibilities

Stakeholder Engagement: Provides meaningful summaries to stakeholders supporting decision-making in a timely fashion. Key to this will be building trust with stakeholders, staying agile and the ability to look beyond the ask to ensure that we enable timely, data-driven decisions. 
Ad Hoc Analysis: The role empowers us to respond swiftly to various data-related reporting, BI, and analytics tasks, providing timely recommendations. This includes addressing ad-hoc requests, resolving data discrepancies, generating executive reports to support decision-making, and ensuring accuracy through reconciliation and validation processes. 
Prepare Reporting and Analytics: Builds, maintains, and improves analytics products in Tableau, Salesforce and Clari to enable automated self-service productivity and performance reporting. Delivers to stakeholder groups and answers related questions. 
Data Exploration: Explores data from different sources to determine productivity trends, correlation, and causation for various areas of the business. Analyze & discover insights related to productivity, performance, and forecasting. Develops an understanding of business dynamics to enable data driven decision-making, process and training optimization and suggests additional analytics opportunities. 
Reviews typical issues around data integrity and works with management to determine what actions to take to resolve them. 

Qualifications

Proven years of related experience preferred. 
Strong analytical skills to work with large amounts of data and server-based data models. 
Advanced user of Tableau with a strong background in reporting & analytics 
Strong experience in MS Excel and PowerPoint 
Excellent written and verbal communication skills.

About the team + role 

The Threat Intelligence team researches threat actors and uses our knowledge to help our partners prioritize the most likely real world threats and advise our leadership on the risks faced by the company. We hunt for attackers on our network and use what we learn to create permanent detection.

As a Senior Threat Intelligence Analyst, you will be the eyes and ears of the security organization, using OSINT and proprietary 3rd party sources to research the latest trends in attacker behavior and communicate about them to partner teams and senior leaders. You will also lead our collaborative hunting program, working with partner teams to proactively seek out potential existing attacker activity. This is a new program that needs your leadership to succeed.

What You’ll Do

Research and track advanced attackers targeting Robinhood and the broader FinTech industry
Analyze, synthesize, and communicate threat intelligence to guide stakeholders' strategic and tactical decisions
Lead a cross-team hunting group that searches for undetected compromises
Provide relevant intelligence to assist in security incident response
Build tools, automate processes, and leverage emerging technologies such as AI to improve efficiency and effectiveness.
Collaborate with industry partners and external security and intelligence communities

What You Bring

B.A., B.S., or M.S. in a technical field, or equivalent experience
4+ years of work experience in cybersecurity threat intelligence, threat research, and/or related functions
Proficiency with SQL, Python scripting, and use of Python notebooks
Experience leading or participating in a cybersecurity hunting program

Quantitative Analyst, Portfolio Analytics

OMERS Total Portfolio Management manages the public markets investment portfolio consisting of fixed income (including government bonds, Inflation-Linked Bonds and public and private credit) and equities, including global public equities, intellectual property and structured investments. The team’s approach is focused on generating current income from high-quality assets and generating a consistent capital return with a lower volatility than the broad markets. We also seek to develop strategic partnerships with best-in-class investors to access credit and other opportunities on a global basis. The OMERS Capital Markets' team is distinguished by its diversity in expertise and experience and its commitment to reliable, lower-risk performance. Our objective is to construct a well-diversified portfolio that will deliver long-term annualized returns in the 6 to 9% range.

Job Description

As a member of the OMERS Total Portfolio Management (TPM) team in Toronto, reporting to the Director, Head of Portfolio Analytics, you will contribute and lead our transformation of how Capital Markets improves investment decision making through data driven insights.

As a Quantitative Analyst, Portfolio Analytics, at OMERS Total Portfolio Management, you will be part of a team that are building world-class analytics and quantitative tools. The role provides the successful candidate with the opportunity to work closely with the Global Credit team, where you will develop and grow your understanding of quantitative and technical tools that drive the development of the systematic components of portfolio management.

As a member of the Portfolio Analytics team, you will be responsible for the following 

Contribute to high-impact initiatives for global Capital Markets investment teams by building & developing platforms that automate internal processes
Design, build, & maintain ETL processes ensuring high quality data is being delivered
Perform cutting-edge AI research driven by a variety of unstructured, semi-structured and structured data sources
Engage with teams across technology, operations and investments to develop and enhance current platforms
Closely collaborate with investment team clients on all stages of project life cycle
Conduct innovative tech, data, and investment research to deliver impactful analytics and insights to Capital Market investment team

You Bring The Following Skills And Qualifications

Bachelor/Master’s degree in computer science, engineering, physics or related field.
2+ years of experience developing and deploying software solutions
Experience with Machine-Learning and Deep Learning, and foundational LLM knowledge
Strong Python programming skills

Our story

Founded in 1962, OMERS is one of Canada’s largest defined benefit pension plans, with $127.4 billion in net assets as at June 30, 2023. OMERS is a jointly-sponsored pension plan, with more than 1,000 participating employers ranging from large cities to local agencies, and over half a million active, deferred and retired members. OMERS members include union and non-union employees of municipalities, school boards, local boards, transit systems, electrical utilities, emergency services and children’s aid societies across Ontario. Contributions to the Plan are funded equally by members and employers. OMERS teams work in Toronto, London, New York, Amsterdam, Luxembourg, Singapore, Sydney and other major cities across North America and Europe – serving members and employers and originating and managing a diversified portfolio of high-quality investments in public markets, private equity, infrastructure and real estate.

OMERS is committed to having a workforce that reflects the communities in which we live and work. We are an equal opportunity employer committed to a barrier-free recruitment and selection process. At OMERS inclusion and diversity means belonging. How we create a sense of belonging is through our employees and our vast network of Employee Resource Groups. Whether you are passionate about gender, pride, or visible minorities, we have groups that are focused on making a difference in all of our lives.
About the job
Affirm is reinventing credit to make it more honest and friendly, giving consumers the flexibility to buy now and pay later without any hidden fees or compounding interest.

We are seeking a highly skilled and experienced Senior Analyst to join our dynamic team, focusing on causal inference and the development of MVP versions of machine learning (ML) models. This role is pivotal in leveraging data science to understand the why behind our data, enabling informed decision-making and driving innovative solutions. The ideal candidate will have a strong background in statistical analysis, causal inference methodologies, and experience in building and iterating on ML models in a fast-paced environment.

What You Will Do

Causal Inference Analysis: Apply advanced causal inference techniques to uncover the underlying mechanisms and effects within our datasets, facilitating a deeper understanding of our data's drivers.
ML Modeling: Develop and refine MVP versions of ML models, focusing on rapid prototyping to test hypotheses and assess potential impact, with an eye towards scalability and integration into larger systems.
Cross-Functional Collaboration: Work closely with product, engineering, and business teams to define problem statements, identify data needs, and implement solutions that align with organizational goals.
Data Strategy Development: Contribute to the creation and execution of a comprehensive data strategy, emphasizing causal analysis and ML applications to support data-driven decision-making.
Insights Communication: Clearly communicate complex analytical findings and model outcomes to non-technical stakeholders, translating data insights into actionable business recommendations.

What We Look For

3+ years of experience in data analysis, with a strong focus on causal inference and ML modeling.
Proficiency in statistical software (R, Python) and familiarity with ML libraries (e.g., scikit-learn, TensorFlow).
Solid understanding of statistical modeling, experimental design, and A/B testing frameworks.
Exceptional analytical, problem-solving, and communication skills.
Bachelor's or Master's degree in Statistics, Computer Science, Economics, or a related quantitative field.
